  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_4e20ab1a-e825-4bed-ab1b-0fc8c7a58e38'

  <span id="freeText2058680118926204574" style="display:none"><i>No safe word can protect the heart</i><br />Infamous erotica author and accomplished dominatrix Nora Sutherlin is doing something utterly out of character: hiding. While her longtime lover, Søren—whose fetishes, if exposed, would be his ruin—is under scrutiny pending a major promotion, Nora's lying low and away from temptation in the lap of luxury.<br /><br />Her host, the wealthy and uninhibited Griffin Fiske, is thrilled to have Nora stay at his country estate, especially once he meets her traveling companion. Young, inexperienced and angelically beautiful, Michael has become Nora's protégé, and this summer with Griffin is going to be his training, where the hazing never ends.<br /><br />But while her flesh is willing, Nora's mind is wandering. To thoughts of Søren, her master, under investigation by a journalist with an ax to grind. And to another man from Nora's past, whose hold on her is less bruising, but whose secrets are no less painful. It's a summer that will prove the old adage: love hurts.</span>

  THE FEELS!!!
</em> Holy intensity!!!! I have tears in my eyes, my heart is racing and full to bursting. Ahhhh!! Yes, a few scenes definitely had me going <em>WhatTheFuckDidIJustRead?!</em> but that's all part of the thrill. This may not </span>

Ok, I did love the first book but <em>now</em> I seriously GET why so many of you absolutely L.O.V.E. this series. I get it. The feels. <em>
  THE FEELS!!!
</em> Holy intensity!!!! I have tears in my eyes, my heart is racing and full to bursting. Ahhhh!! Yes, a few scenes definitely had me going <em>WhatTheFuckDidIJustRead?!</em> but that's all part of the thrill. This may not be a romance series, but my gosh is there ever <strong>LOVE</strong> on such a <em>strong</em> level. And LAYERS. Layers upon layers to this intricate story. I'm in pure awe. This is 5 STARS!!!<br><br>Note: this is not a standalone, you must read The Siren (review: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1I3176u">http://bit.ly/1I3176u</a>) first. I'm going to keep this review pretty much spoiler-free so anyone can read it but naturally it'll make more sense after reading The Siren.<br><br>The first page of this book alone hooked me right into the story! Ha!! This book is just so <em>bold</em> and I love it!! I have so many quotes highlighted (they're all at the bottom of the review though).<br><br>I'd spent most of the first book eyeing Søren warily, but I did really start to warm up to him in the beginning of this book especially. Sadist or no, there was no doubt that he genuinely loved Nora. But juuuuuuust when I started to think that maybe I could join #TeamSøren, he did something to her that, in his defence, she totally was okay with, but made my insides shrivel up into a little ball while my poor mind was just like <em>WTFJustHappened?! Did I really read that?! </em> So... that put me back on the fence with him. Ish. The thing is that I do really like him. He's an infinitely complex character that I truly believe is one of the good guys... but, I'm still rooting for Wesley (and I have from the start). Gah, I'm <em>so</em> rooting for Wesley even though a part of me fears it could never work out between him and Nora. Still, I harbor a secret hope!<br><br>There's a very fine line in my opinion between being a monster and being a sadist. Søren is a sadist -- he becomes sexually aroused by causing pain to others. Soren doesn't ever take what isn't willingly given to him, and he's extraordinarily careful to stay within the boundaries of his submissive's wishes. <em>That</em> is what separates him... but that damn line is just so fine that the whole thing relies purely on <em>trust</em> and even though I like him, it does make me a uncomfortable that he <em>has</em> to cause pain <em>to</em> get aroused.<br><br>The story in this book begins with Søren's position at the church coming under scrutiny as he's considered for a promotion and so, to avoid any questioning, he sends Nora away to the countryside to spend time at Griffin's mansion. And he also sends Michael with her (a young, troubled sub who we met in The Siren and who was such an amazing character!) to train him over the summer months.<br><br>I find the whole lack of jealousy between Søren and Nora fascinating. He'll literally tell her to go  sleep with someone else, but it won't bother him at all because he knows full well that she belongs to <em>him </em>and his heart belongs to her. It's this incredibly strong commitment mixed with equally strong detachment.<br><br>Haha I definitely went through a lot of ups and downs and conflicting emotions and questioning the characters and myself and how I felt about various things but ultimately I just LOVED the story!<br><br>Griffin was totally awesome! I liked him from the first book even though we'd just seen him briefly but he really shone here! I totally fell for his playful, informal nature. He was the charming, kinky bad boy of the Underground and the whole storyline with Michael totally made me <em>swoooooon!! </em>What intensity and beauty there was there!! And that scene at the end where Griffin had that big confrontation and all those things to <em>you know who</em>.... OMG!! Bad <em>ass!!!</em> I highlighted endlessly! It was GOLD.<br><br>This book had a ton of reveals about Nora and Søren's pasts. Holy crap is Søren history ever messed up. Like... shockingly, disturbingly, heart-breakingly so.  But learning it has made me understand him more. Oh and we got to see more of Kingsley (YAY!) and the little bits that we've seen have me desperate to know more about him. Like, the wrist thing? Ahhh, I can't wait for more of his character!<br><br>And you know I've been rooting for  Wes from the start but after <em>that scene</em> at 75%, I just.... OMG. Oh. Em. Gee. Gah. I know, I know, <em>I know</em> that Søren loves Nora too but the <em>way</em> Wesley loves her just tugs each and every one of my heart strings!!!!! I'm sorry #TeamSoren, I get that you all love him (and I like him too, I really do) but I'm #TeamWesley all the way!!! Especially after that scene. THAT SCENE!!!!! I mean really.... First -- PURE FUCKING AMAZING WRITING!!! Second -- holy intensity!!! Third -- I seriously can't handle those feels. I can't. Dammit. SO MANY FEELS!!!!! And just... I LOVE WESLEY!!!!!! *sob*<br><br>And I just want to point out that Wes is the <em>only</em> guy that Nora has actually shown real jealousy for. No one else in their world (including her) seems to even have the jealousy gene (heh) but even the mere suggestion of Wes being with someone else  made her heart hurt. <em>There's something there, people!!</em><br><br>That being said, I'm kind of rooting for <em>everyone</em> honestly. I don't think there's a single character I've met yet that I didn't like so ... I'm rooting for everyone to find their happy ending :)<br><br>I want to note that I'm generally very wary of religion in books because so often it feels a little "preachy", but I really want to applaud this author for the way she has incorporated this huge religious aspect into this series in a way that only ever seems like she's showing us what the characters' beliefs are and that's it. I think she's handled it very tastefully and it's something I've been really impressed with overall.<br><br>This is such a richly layered story. Yes, it's extremely erotic but the beauty of it is that each sex scene only serves to support the story or drive it forward. And not only are these extremely graphic and sensual scenes extremely well written, but they always serve a purpose. In my opinion, <em>this</em> is erotica done right.<br><br>And I stand by what I said earlier that this is not a romance series but <em>oh my holy heavens</em> is there ever some of the deepest, strongest, most intense LOVE I've ever read. It's just gorgeous!<br><br>In so many ways this series is literally the opposite of what I'd usually read or even recommend on my blog but this seems to be the exception to every one of my rules because I am absolutely LOVING this story. If you have any worries holding you back from starting it, I'd honestly suggest not overthinking it. Just dive right in and let the story show you what it is. It might not be for you, but if you remain very open minded and accepting, you might fall in love with it too! I'd say it's definitely worth a shot!<br><br>I, for one, am beyond addicted to this series and will be starting the next book right away!<br><br><strong>Rating: 5 STARS!! Contemporary erotica.</strong><br><br>My review of book #1: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1I3176u">http://bit.ly/1I3176u</a><br>________________________________________<br><br><b>SERIES READING ORDER: </b><br>Book #1: The Siren <br>Book #2: The Angel<br>Book #3: The Prince<br>Book #4: The Mistress<br>Book #5: The Saint<br>Book #6: The King<br>Book #7: The Virgin<br>Book #8: The Queen<br>________________________________________<br><br><b>MY FAVORITE QUOTES: </b><br>Note: I've "hidden" these in a spoiler tag but they are NOT spoilers. I only hid them because there are a lot and I thought it would be annoying to just have them out there. Have a look if you want, it's perfectly safe :)<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ “Happy now?”<br>Soren pulled her to him and ran his fingers over her cheek.<br>“You’re here. Of course I am.”<br>________________________<br>Kingsley had a fascinating relationship with the press — fascinating in the way the sack of Rome by invading Barbarian hordes was fascinating. A reporter once threatened to run a story exposing one of Kingsley’s clients — an internationally renowned human rights attorney — as a transvestite with multiple sexual fetishes. Two nights before the story ran, a sex tape that the reporter and her husband made played on an endless loop on every computer in their six-year-old’s exclusive private school. The video was unremovable. All two hundred computers had to be scrapped and replaced.<br>The story never ran.<br>________________________<br>“Out of the question,” Soren said. “I know how you behave in other countries. That you are still allowed a passport is one of the universe’s great mysteries.”<br>________________________<br>“You are my heart,” he said. He’s said those very words to her that morning. But that morning they’d sounded affectionate and playful. Now he said them as if he were stating a fact of anatomy. “I will not lose you.”<br>________________________<br>“She wanted him to make love to her again, but the moment had passed. A true sadist, Soren could only become aroused by inflicting pain and humiliation.”<br>________________________<br>“Nora reached out and touched the wound just over Soren’s heart. A superficial cut, it would heal in just days. The wounds underneath, however, were old and scarified and likely would never completely heal. Scar tissue, she’d once read, was the strongest of tissues. Maybe Soren’s heart was so strong because it was so scarred.”<br>________________________<br>“No interruptions for the next couple of hours, please. My guest and I will be fucking. Two hours, Nora?”<br>“At least,” she agreed.<br>“Better make it three, Alfred.” Griffin shifted Nora higher on his shoulder and continued up the stairs.<br>“This is going to be a long summer, isn’t it?” she asked.<br>“Eight and a half inches long, if you’ll recall.”<br>________________________<br>“He was damaged, dangerous and dead sexy —Kingsley’s favourite combination.”<br>________________________<br>“I’m so in love with him I can’t even think straight. Which is fine since obviously I’m not straight. And neither is he.” <br>________________________<br>“I want you inside me,” he said simply … “I will beg you for it if you order me to. And I’ll beg you for it even if you don’t.” <br>________________________<br>“The jealous haters could have her spreader bars and her signature red riding crop when they pried them out of her cold, dead hands.”<br>________________________<br>“Winter,” she finally said, “can be beautiful and so cruel. Cruel and cold. And if you live in the presence of winter you never have summer.” Nora stepped close to him and put her nose at his cheek. “You smell like summer. Like clean laundry hanging out in the sun. That’s an amazing smell too.”<br>________________________<br>“My confession begins,” Father S said, “as the confessions of many men begin — with three words.”<br>“Father, forgive me?” Michael hazarded a guess.<br>Father S sighed.<br>“I met Eleanor.”<br>________________________<br>“A really good dominant can put the fear of God into a sub with a whisper. Soren certainly can.”<br>“Soren can put the fear of God into a sub by just showing up,” Griffin said with barely concealed envy.<br>________________________<br>“Can I call you Mick? Michael’s too formal. I’m not formal. You’re lucky I’ve even got pants on today.” <br>________________________<br>“Your mind is both fascinating and repulsive.”<br>________________________<br>Until now Michael had always thought of kink as something dark and dangerous, something for fetishists and freaks like him. Now it suddenly dawned on him. BDSM was a game —a game where both players won.<br>________________________<br>Just looking at her, feeling himself falling under her spell, he could easily understand how men would mortgage their souls just to be able to kiss the toe of her boot.<br>________________________<br>“You’ve never met Soren. He’s a very good person. Best man I’ve ever known.”<br>“You told me about him. Good men don’t hit women.”<br>“Good men only hit the women who want to be hit.”<br>“Women shouldn’t want to be hit.”<br>“Then that’s her problem, not his, right?”<br>________________________<br>“I love her,” Wesley whispered. “I love her more than my own life, and you…” He finally met Soren’s eyes. “You hurt her.”<br>Soren nodded.<br>“I do.”<br>________________________<br>“No, she and I never had sex. That’s true. But we had love, real love that didn’t take anything out of us, that didn’t bruise or break us. I loved her without hurting her.” <br>________________________<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of <span id="freeTextContainer14129796896626438046"><b>★★★★★ 5++++ MANY WATERS STARS!! ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418747229i/12887525.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"This is going to be a long summer, isn't it?"<br/>"Eight and a half inches long if you'll recall."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>I usually don't do casting in my graphics but when it comes to the Original Sinners, one does not simply skip out on them. SO VOILA ABOVE MY CASTING ♥ Also, thanks Allison for the constant spamming of hot delish men pictures that allowed my imagination to explode in ecstasy as I read! <br/><br/><b>Now let's take a moment and appreciate how f*cking awesome Griffin is.</b> </span>
  <span id="freeText14129796896626438046" style="display:none"><b>★★★★★ 5++++ MANY WATERS STARS!! ★★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418747229i/12887525.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"This is going to be a long summer, isn't it?"<br>"Eight and a half inches long if you'll recall."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I usually don't do casting in my graphics but when it comes to the Original Sinners, one does not simply skip out on them. SO VOILA ABOVE MY CASTING ♥ Also, thanks Allison for the constant spamming of hot delish men pictures that allowed my imagination to explode in ecstasy as I read! <br><br><b>Now let's take a moment and appreciate how f*cking awesome Griffin is.</b> Seriously, Tiffany Reisz continues to add more and more men to my list of people who I'd gladly have my way with six ways to Sunday. The moment his glorious entry was all <i>"wearing nothing but a kilt and Doc Marten boots"</i>, I knew I'd be a complete goner with this man. And good lord, his humor is to dieeeee forrrrr!! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Can I call you Mick? Michael's too formal. I'm not formal. You're lucky I've even got pants on today.”</i>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Is your butler's name really Alfred?"<br>"No, it's Jamison, I think. Can't remember. I changed it to Alfred years ago. My first crush on a dude was batman."</i>
</blockquote> <br>And holy baby jeebus that is <b>Søren.</b> My love for that Godlike man cannot get any deeper than I last met him. Is he a sadist that scares me? <b>Yes.</b> Does that completely turn me on? <b>YES.</b> Everytime Søren utters anything, I give my 300% attention to that man, his character truly does make heads turn and leaves you holding your breath. He exudes a persona that intimidates you but yet leaves you utterly captivated by him. And you can just <b>
  <i>feel</i>
</b> the depth of his love for Nora everytime he speaks about her, DAMN YOU NORA YOU LUCKY BEECH. <br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>“My confession begins,” Father S said, “as the confessions of many men begin– <b>with three words.</b>”<br>“Father, forgive me?” Michael hazarded a guess.<br><b>“I met Eleanor.”</b></i>
</blockquote><br>Again, I don't intend to reveal any spoilery plots on this book and series in my review but I can definitely say that <b>each book seriously gets better than the last. </b> A COMPLETE PAGE-TURNER. <b>TR's writing screams perfection on every level!!</b> Even with multiple perspectives going on in this book, what a seamless flow from one to another. Plus the chain effect of multiple events and how it all connects, it leaves me mindblown. <b>I AM IN COMPLETE AWE WITH THIS LADY'S WRITING SKILLS.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429781ra/861211.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>What's even more perfect is we all get <b>some backstory</b> on most of them; Søren, Kingsley, Nora, Wes. Everyone gets an equal shine of the spotlight without focusing heavily on only one, it was brilliantly balanced out throughout the book. I love how we got to see things progressed for Michael and oh my, those MM/MMF scenes ;D I'd gladly have an encore of these anytime! MORE PLEASE. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Let’s get on with it. Pick a position. Trust me, no matter how acrobatic, we can do it.”<br>“No wall sex though, please,” Griffin requested … “Nora’s a lot heavier than she looks.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Seriously ladies, GRIFFIN IS ALL KINDS OF AWESOME. <br><br>But most of all...that ending there. <b>OH MY GOD. THAT. ENDING.</b> Off to the next one NOW!!! <br></span>

<div id="review_336801143" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/336801143" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/336801143?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2012</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer928923873373921235">FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED.<br/><br/><br/>My review contains spoilers for The Siren so, if you haven’t read that, I suggest you read no further.<br/><br/>So, a highly anticipated sequel to The Siren and I’m happy to say that it doesn’t disappoint and really does even surpass its predecessor. All our favourite characters are back, embracing their kink, living unashamedly in their sexy underworld. I think this is more playful than The Siren, not as angsty, the characters are all, mostly, having fun. It’s a blast and it just b</span>
  <span id="freeText928923873373921235" style="display:none">FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED.<br><br><br>My review contains spoilers for The Siren so, if you haven’t read that, I suggest you read no further.<br><br>So, a highly anticipated sequel to The Siren and I’m happy to say that it doesn’t disappoint and really does even surpass its predecessor. All our favourite characters are back, embracing their kink, living unashamedly in their sexy underworld. I think this is more playful than The Siren, not as angsty, the characters are all, mostly, having fun. It’s a blast and it just blew me away.<br><br>We join Nora and Søren almost a year after the events of The Siren – she has returned to her sadist master. He owns her; body and soul, and they are deeply in love, deeply into S&amp;M and blissfully happy. Her only sadness is the loss of Wesley.<br><br>Søren is being considered for a promotion to bishop, a position he doesn’t want because he knows it will probably end his relationship with Nora, and a reporter is sniffing around him looking for scandal so he decides to send Nora away for the summer and tells her to take Michael, the eponymous Angel, upstate to stay with Griffin Fiske.<br><br>Griffin – super rich trustfund baby, switch and playboy extraordinaire, ex-drug addict, rambunctious puppy of the kink scene and lovable rogue. He has a butler he calls Alfred who quite clearly hates his guts and has the best lines in the book and is looking forward to a summer of Nora submitting to him. Søren will happily share her but no one is allowed to beat her or hurt her in any way – that sadistic pleasure is reserved just for him.<br><br>Michael is sent to stay with them and Søren instructs Nora to train him as a submissive. Michae just about broke my heart. Only 17, he has already survived one suicide attempt when his parents realised what his sexual tendencies are – he’s deeply submissive and Søren, having saved his life, is determined that Michael will embrace his kink and can think of no one better than Nora, a world famous dominatrix, to train him. He thinks himself in love with Nora after the events of The Siren – he’s such an innocent, so ready to be taken advantage of. He will need someone as powerful as Nora to take control and care of him and guide him to more self-awareness and acceptance. This is truly a coming of age story for Michael and I very much enjoyed his journey and his growth.<br><br>So what follows for Nora is a summer of darkly delicious and deviant sex Chez Griff while Søren deals with his situation back at the church. <br><br>Søren was such a revelation for me in this book. After The Siren, I was fairly wary of him but after reading The Angel, I just adore him. He is a sadist of the highest order, only causing someone physical pain can arouse him and he and Nora indulge in some extreme edgeplay before she goes away that is most definitely not for the faint-hearted. We learn a whole lot more about his past, his family, his motivations – I defy you not to love him and his actions by the end of the book. He’s enigmatic, Machiavellian, a bone deep sadist and also pretty damn good at the day job, as it turns out. He’s a paradox – a sadist who can only achieve sexual arousal by inflicting pain and yet a pacifist, deeply concerned with the welfare of those closest to his heart and his flock. <br><br>Another of my favourites is back too – that wicked Frenchman Kingsley “have you ever had sex in the back of a Rolls Royce” Edge, flashing those gorgeous dark eyes, using his considerable wealth and influence and reducing women to submissive puddles when the words ‘Ma Cherie’ roll off his tongue. He has an important role to play here too. God, I am so in lust with him!<br><br>Wesley makes only small appearances but it turns out that he’s been rather economical with the truth in the past and we learn more about him and he will obviously have a much bigger role to play in The Prince. He’s still in love with Nora, no one else will do even though he does try, and Nora still loves him. He is her one regret and she misses him deeply.<br><br>This may not be classic romance but true and honest love is definitely to be found here in more places than one. These people are overtly sexual, unashamedly embracing their darker sides and Nora is, once again, a formidable, dangerous, beautiful central character. There are not many heroines written as strongly as her in erotic fiction. Once again, I found myself lost in Tiffany Reisz’s beautiful prose – she has a style that seems to transport you from reality, straight into her world and I just lost myself.<br><br>So, this is just a few more chapters in the lives of our kinksters – we learn a lot more about the central characters and are able to answer questions left unanswered by The Siren and truly get to understand their motivations better. We know them all so much better by the end and the ending is a shocker – how could you do it to us Queen Tiff?? It left me salivating for The Prince which I suspect will show a return to the darker side.<br><br>Another 5 star piece of erotica<br><br>This is how I see Nora<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378897i/734820._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>With thanks to Harlequin via Netgalley for my ARC</i><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6440784939398783614"><i>Adult review for erotic content.</i><br/><br/>I think I'd rather be doing laundry than writing this review right now. I wish I were kidding. It's hard to write reviews for books when you want to emphasize what you did like while not completely avoiding what you didn't like. <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You told me about him. Good men don't hit women."<br/>"Good men only hit the women who want to be hit."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Can we somehow put this on an advertisement poster for BDSM? Maybe if we did, the subject wouldn't freak people out so much.<br/><br/>So..</span>
  <span id="freeText6440784939398783614" style="display:none"><i>Adult review for erotic content.</i><br /><br />I think I'd rather be doing laundry than writing this review right now. I wish I were kidding. It's hard to write reviews for books when you want to emphasize what you did like while not completely avoiding what you didn't like. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You told me about him. Good men don't hit women."<br />"Good men only hit the women who want to be hit."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Can we somehow put this on an advertisement poster for BDSM? Maybe if we did, the subject wouldn't freak people out so much.<br /><br />So...book 2 was a little less depressing and a little more kinky. I probably prefer it that way if you want to know the truth. Kink I can handle. Somber moments in the middle of my erotica, not so much. Just the sight of a Megan Hart book can give me hives because I know I'm going to spend less time turned on and more time bummed out. Thankfully, I wasn't on the depression train for this book. Just a warning though if you haven't read my review for book 1 - if there is any possibility that you might be bothered by religion and sex crossing paths (not in a blatantly offensive way but more in the aspect of two worlds colliding), you might be better off steering clear. <br /><br />*takes a second to stretch*<br /><br />Uh...yeah. Still not sure I want to write this review. I already know that everyone's going to be all, "ahhhmaaazing" and 5 star <i>The Angel</i> because the book is an interesting and complex read. The writing is still exceptionally polished and the characters are all multi-faceted. I can find absolutely no fault in this area.<br /><br />I'm sure my friends are going to give me the glare-down because I didn't rate the book 5 stars. <br /><br /><i>However, I have a horrible confession to make....</i> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I really don't like Nora. As in, I borderline hate the woman and the decisions she makes. Sometimes in life we just don't get everything we want. I think someone forgot to tell her that. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Yep. I said it. Which kind of sucks hard, considering that she is kind of a big character. If you want to know why I'll just leave it at "too personal." Sometimes, being able to relate to a character is <i>not</i> a good thing.<br /><br /><b>But I still love Wesley.</b> And now I love Michael and Griffin (you will have to pry the image of Griffin in a kilt and docs out of my brain with a crowbar because that pretty picture ain't going anywhere). And I don't completely hate Soren (he appeared in a dream riding a unicorn - another great mental pic there). So it's all good.<br /><br />The kink itself didn't push any boundaries of mine but I could see where there might be some comfort zone issues for someone who is new to the genre. If anything, I found myself assessing the characters and their interactions with each other more than I did their sexual preferences. When erotica is given more plot than play, I'm more likely to treat it like I would any other mainstream book, which means less allowances for fantasy sake. If characters act in such a way that I'd not like them in a real world setting, I'm more likely to take notice.<br /><br /><b>Overall feelings?</b><br />I like that there are more characters coming into the picture for me to bond with. At least this way, I can focus on the stories I am more interested in and push back small annoyances. The anticipation for book 3 will be great because it means even more <i>Wesley</i> time! Sure, I'll be continuing on with the series. Lastly, it was nice to see some offbeat and unexpected humor pop up in a few places.<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Noah's ark nursery decor. I'm not religious like you and the mistress, but if I'm not mistaken Noah's ark was about the destruction of the entire world, right?"<br />"Right," Michael agreed.<br />"Might as well decorate with the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse."<br />Shrugging, Michael looked at the walls now painted an elegant light blue.<br />"Kids like ponies."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br /><i>This book was provided from the publisher through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1882163668?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--">Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=mm-romance">mm-romance</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1882163668" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7746852042309280771"><b>RATING: 5+ "Many Waters..." Hearts!! :) <3</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Many waters cannot quench love, Nor will rivers overflow it.” Song of Solomon 8:7 </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><i>The Angel</i> is simply erotic romance at its finest. There is something sinfully beautiful about this masterful world Ms. Reisz has created, the characters that inhabit it, and their compelling stories. This book invoked raw emotions in me I can't explain even if I tried.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Love is the open wound that you hope never heals.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Nora, Søren and Kingsley are</span>
  <span id="freeText7746852042309280771" style="display:none"><b>RATING: 5+ "Many Waters..." Hearts!! :) &lt;3</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Many waters cannot quench love, Nor will rivers overflow it.” Song of Solomon 8:7 </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><i>The Angel</i> is simply erotic romance at its finest. There is something sinfully beautiful about this masterful world Ms. Reisz has created, the characters that inhabit it, and their compelling stories. This book invoked raw emotions in me I can't explain even if I tried.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Love is the open wound that you hope never heals.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Nora, Søren and Kingsley are ever present in this book, but I want to talk about two characters that truly made me understand—even a pinch of—this world and lifestyle: Griffin and Michael. Griffin is hilarious, easy-going and protective to the core. Michael is a young man, broken by all the cruelties life has given, yet still not weak as he tries to understand and take control (relative to his desire to submit ;) of his life and his desires. His first step into the unknown and his utter determination to grasp the very thing that which makes him whole is awe-inspiring and relatable. And the two of them together are the epitome of a soul-deep friendship, new beginnings, and an everlasting, irrevocable love. I LOVED both of them so much, and LOVED their love for one another!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “I want to own you,”...<br />“You already do.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />The ending is surprising to say the least, and because of it, I concede; I am beginning to actually like and understand Søren. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Winter," she finally said, "can be so beautiful and so cruel. Cruel and cold. And if you live in the presence of winter you never have summer." Nora stepped close to him and put her nose at his cheek. "You smell like summer. Like clean laundry hanging out in the sun. That’s an amazing smell too.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Definitely my fave, as of yet, of the series!<br /><br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>Posted: January 28, 2017</b>
</i></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1133406336" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1133406336" />
    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1133406336?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6285155-eda?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1133406336" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16114846650021711487"><b>
  <i>** 4-4,5 “<u>Jeg elsker dig, du er mit hjerte</u>” STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No safe word can protect the heart.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419464999ra/13073156.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>Once again, I am lost in Tiffany Reisz’s dangerously dark and confusingly erotic world.</b>
</i> I’ve been having dreams about this book since I finished it 2 days ago and find myself thinking about the characters in the middle of the day, out of nowhere. This woman has become one of my favorite authors <b>EVER</b> so quickly, and has practically ruined me for all the other erotica books out there with h</span>
  <span id="freeText16114846650021711487" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>** 4-4,5 “<u>Jeg elsker dig, du er mit hjerte</u>” STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No safe word can protect the heart.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419464999ra/13073156.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Once again, I am lost in Tiffany Reisz’s dangerously dark and confusingly erotic world.</b>
</i> I’ve been having dreams about this book since I finished it 2 days ago and find myself thinking about the characters in the middle of the day, out of nowhere. This woman has become one of my favorite authors <b>EVER</b> so quickly, and has practically ruined me for all the other erotica books out there with her master writing skills.<br><br>From the moment you read the first sentence on the first page, you get sucked into the story and all you can do is try to connect the dots…the tiny details here and there, seemingly unimportant but rather crucial for the backbone of the story. Some of the clues I could catch, some of them I could notice only when the mystery was already uncovered, but I was left in awe <b>
  <i>every single time</i>
</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389759305ra/8053358.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let’s start with the highlight of the book: <b>Griffin Fiske</b>’s butler, <b>Alfred</b>. Yes, he was my favorite thing about this book! <i>No, I’m serious you guys, don’t laugh!!</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Alfred, are you looking up my skirt?”<br><br>“Master Griffin, I would marry my own mother for the excuse to stab my eyes out with her brooches rather than see anything under your kilt.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>See? He’s freakin' hilarious! The love between him and his “master” is palpable…LOL.<br><br>Speaking of <b>Griffin Fiske</b>… <b>HOW GODDAMN PERFECT IS THAT GUY, RIGHT?!</b> If I wasn’t already undeniably in love with <i>Father Søren</i>, I’d shamelessly fall in love with this man in a heartbeat! His sense of humor, his authority, his bravery and honesty…it’s all so mesmerizing. Oh and let’s not forget that he likes to strut around the house in his boxers!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391853579ra/8466558.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Most importantly though, I loved the way he silently and slowly fell in love with a certain broken <b>Angel</b>… I loved how fiercely he could love someone and how willing he was to fight for that person. When Nora asks him, <b>
  <i>“That bad, huh?”</i>
</b> and he replies, looking adoringly at the person he loves, <b>
  <i>“Yeah…that bad.”</i>
</b>, my heart filled with something warm and heavy for him! ♥<br><br>Let's move on to <b>Kingsley Edge</b>… THE ANSWER TO MY PRAYERS! Thank God for his presence in this story! There’s a reason for my sudden fascination with this sexy Frenchman and it’s not just because he asks questions like <b>
  <i>“Have you ever had sex in the back of a Rolls Royce?”</i>
</b> to everyone who get inside his…well, Rolls Royce, and because everytime he says <b>
  <i>“ma chérie”</i>
</b> my panties melt and disappear. No, it has another, <i>much deeper</i> reason behind it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I've wondered a time or two if I love le prêtre more than you do, chérie. Now I know I do.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419366484ra/13046594.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Father Marcus Lennox Stearns... My <b>Søren</b>. After this book, I know I’ve made the right choice to see the light inside him, ignoring the darker and scarier exterior. <i>He has reasons.</i> He has scars, so deep. Take off your glasses of judgement and look at him with naked eyes. You’ll see his inner beauty, I know you will...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419464597ra/13072815.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Wesley Railey</b> was absent for most of the book, but he had a VERY important part in the story. I just want to say, I admire his naivety and his big heart, <i>but I am absolutely disappointed with him.</i> The cruel and hurtful words he used while talking to Søren… <i>So judgemental and prejudiced.</i> And rather ironic too, wouldn’t you agree? He insists on always seeing the <b>good</b> and <b>pure</b> in Nora, but refuses to try to understand Søren. He is 20 years old now, but he was acting like a 12-year-old who stumped his feet because he lost his favorite toy. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419464597ra/13072816.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And lastly…<b>Nora Sutherlin</b>. The woman that I absolutely loathed while reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10970532.The_Siren__The_Original_Sinners___1_" title="The Siren (The Original Sinners, #1) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">The Siren</a>, not because of her <b>wicked</b> ways, but because of her selfishness. The woman that has loved a man that <b>needs</b> to hurt her, nearly twenty years. The woman that kept dreaming of a boy with <i>big brown eyes with flecks of gold in them</i> in every chapter of this book. The woman that repeated 105 times that she is still in love with her Priest and that she will <b>always</b> come back to him. The woman that climaxed with another man, but with the name of that boy who played Battleship with her, on her lips. <br><br><i>
  <b>You see, I don’t believe someone can be in love with two different people at the same time.</b>
</i> Especially after my boyfriend of 2,5 years told me “he carried a heart with two women’s names engraved on it” after getting caught cheating on me. I didn’t believe that boy could love me and someone else both then and I still don’t.<br><br>So yeah… I don’t understand <b>Nora Sutherlin</b>. But…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419384702ra/13049874.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>…so I’ve decided to let go of my sharp hatred and fury towards her. In my mind, she is a woman that has fallen out of love with a man that, at some point, became just too much to handle, and she found love again in the arms of an innocent. I believe she is ready to give herself <i>“heart, body and soul”</i> to the boy that gave her the pajama pants with little penguins on it, but just isn’t ready to let go of her 18 years of submission and sacrifice.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“<u>Winter</u> can be so beautiful and so cruel. Cruel and cold. And if you live in the presence of winter you never have summer. You smell like <u>summer</u>. Like clean laundry hanging out in the sun. That’s an amazing smell too.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Nora has been living in <b>winter</b> for years. She needs to try <b>summer</b> now. <i>And as much as it breaks my heart, I get it.</i> I even wish she never gets bored of <b>summer</b>. I wish she never craves <b>winter</b> again.<br><br><i><b>Winter</b> is better off without her anyway.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Eleanor, if you have any mercy in that dark heart of yours, when you leave right now, you will walk and not run.”<br><br>(...)And Nora didn't walk and she didn't crawl and she didn't fly.<br><br><u>She ran.</u></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>
  <blockquote>♥ BuddyRead with my lovely pal Sandyღ ♥<br>Thank you so much for tolerating the overflow of messages and complaints about Nora, baby!</blockquote>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16114846650021711487" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer641996970" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9862276152799598119"><b>5 HOT KINKY STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425472ra/849192.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>OMG I want all of them!!!Can I have them???????It was amazing!!!</b><br/><br/>Definately Tiffany Reisz became one of my favourite author!!!She manage to make me think Soren not so bad at all!! <br/> <br/>In this book not only do we have the chance to reconnect with the characters we fell in love in the first book but also we have the chance to get to know them all better!!<br/>I love all the characters!!They feel so real to me!!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849193._SY540_.jpg' width='200' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849194._SY540_.jpg' width='200' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Nora is back in her submissive role to Søren...<br/>You can just see and feel how</span>
  <span id="freeText9862276152799598119" style="display:none"><b>5 HOT KINKY STARS!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425472ra/849192.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>OMG I want all of them!!!Can I have them???????It was amazing!!!</b><br><br>Definately Tiffany Reisz became one of my favourite author!!!She manage to make me think Soren not so bad at all!! <br> <br>In this book not only do we have the chance to reconnect with the characters we fell in love in the first book but also we have the chance to get to know them all better!!<br>I love all the characters!!They feel so real to me!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849193._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849194._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Nora is back in her submissive role to Søren...<br>You can just see and feel how much Søren loves her and cares for her..<br><br> <b>“Jeg elsker dig. Du er mit hjerte.”<br> I love you. You are my heart.</b><br> <br> <b>"You belong to me...always."<br> "Always"</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425472ra/849195.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I even loved Soren after this book and I NEVER would have guessed that was possible!!!He was the only character that I truly disliked after the first book!But now what can I say about him???He was so freaking sweet and caring.He has offered to give up the priesthood for Nora and be there for her but it wasn’t enough for her and now we know why it wasn’t enough..<br>Nora is devoted to him and that will never change...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849196.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There is a reporter Sussane who try to expose Søren and his horrific past and fetishes..<br>To avoid being an even bigger liability,Nora goes into hiding and takes the young Michael with her to Griffin Fiske's estate...<br><br>So the three have a lovely summer holiday in which Nora undertakes to train Michael...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849197.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425472i/849198.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I love both guys!!They are cute!Griffin is such a fun character and Michael is a sweetheart with a beautiful soul and like most teenagers he doesn’t know what to do with the fantasies that plague him...<br><br><br><br><b>"I want to own you" Griffin whispered into Michael's ear. Michael smiled and for the first time in his life knew exactly what to say and how to say it. "You already do"</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425472ra/849199.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Nora misses Søren and secretly misses Wesley..<br><br><br>We also see a little more of Kingsley.He is very intriguing!I have had a hard time trying to figure out Kingsley.He had a huge secret exposed in this book..But we will learn more for him in the next book!<br>(I can't wait to learn more about him!! :)) )<br><br> <br><br>Nora is still Nora and I love her!She's hilarious and sexy as hell!!<br><br> <br>This book was just plain amazing!!It's absolutely one of my favourite books!!! <br><br><br><a href="http://24.media.tumblr.com/d4cef36663ab7c3ef851c7fd5e7256ec/tumblr_mpv3mfjHwD1s9ajydo1_500.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer980498978" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1219751766798086108"><b>6 hilariously kinky STARS!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418991765i/12962106.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><blockquote>
<b><i>“Hey, bad girl,” came the deep, sexy voice of The Griffin himself. “Can’t believe the Pope let you out of the Vatican.”</i></b> </blockquote><br/><br/><i>**Buddy-Re-Read December 2014 with my girls Jasmine, Supreet and Eda...well sort of...for some reason we got a little lost and read it at different paces. Uppps. Anyway, I tweaked my original review a little, added some graphics and thoughts. Enjoy. ;D</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
<b><i>“Come on in. Let's get this orgy started.”</i></b> </blockquote><br/><br/>And we have the winner for this month’s stay up all night</span>
  <span id="freeText1219751766798086108" style="display:none"><b>6 hilariously kinky STARS!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418991765i/12962106.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>“Hey, bad girl,” came the deep, sexy voice of The Griffin himself. “Can’t believe the Pope let you out of the Vatican.”</i></b> </blockquote><br><br><i>**Buddy-Re-Read December 2014 with my girls Jasmine, Supreet and Eda...well sort of...for some reason we got a little lost and read it at different paces. Uppps. Anyway, I tweaked my original review a little, added some graphics and thoughts. Enjoy. ;D</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>“Come on in. Let's get this orgy started.”</i></b> </blockquote><br><br>And we have the winner for this month’s stay up all night and read until your eyes cross contest. I can’t put this series down and I damn well don’t want to.<br>In my opinion you have to be fairly open minded to read these books, even by erotica and dark read standards. <i>(**little sidenote after the re-read...I think I read a few more dark reads since I first wrote this...it's not that shocking in hindsight. LOL)</i> But once you commit to the characters and the world they live in there is no going back. I’m certain I will never pick up a BDSM book and read it without comparing it with a Tiffany Reisz book. <i>(**now that on the other hand is spot on)</i><br><br>As it turns out there is a difference between SSC and RACK. ;)<br><br>Besides being very naughty, well written and addictive, The Angel was also very educational and insightful. A lot of the unanswered questions from The Siren and some huge gaps in the timeline get filled in and man is that some story telling. Tiffany Reisz sure knows what she’s doing.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Bless me, Father, for I have sinned. It has been…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>One of my first concerns was what happened with Zach and do we see him again. I have to confess my priorities can be a bit controversial, but that’s just how I live my life. So, to appease all minds...we get some -very little but still- Zach. That alone in my book deserves 6 Stars. As I said, warped priorities.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419280567i/13026149.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No safe word can protect the heart.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>To the story. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13548075-the-angel" rel="nofollow noopener">The Angel</a> picks up where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10970532-the-siren" rel="nofollow noopener">The Siren</a> ends...well, just one minor thing, a year has passed. Nora is finally back with the sadistic blond hunk of a man. No complains there.<br><br>Wes is somewhere else. Major plus! I like Wes well enough but I don’t like him enough to care what happens to him either way.<br><br>Clue in a possible promotion for our favourite priest, a nosy reporter who by the way made me nervous like no one else in this book and a little Angel in search for love and acceptance. And of course Griffin, Nora and Michael penned up in a mansion over the summer. Recipe for a masterpiece.<br><br>And I'm doing happy dances around the house...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>”I’ve hurt people. I’ve hurt them badly. I’ve left permanent<br>scars on some clients. Some outer scars. Some inner. But all<br>that pain I’ve inflicted…it was all consensual. I’ve never hurt anyone without their permission. All I’m saying, Ms. Kanter, is…” Sutherlin leaned forward and pressed the lightest, softest, most terrifying kiss onto Suzanne’s lips before pulling back an inch and whispering, “There’s a first time for everything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Nora continues to be the strongest and most fearless book heroine I’ve seen in a long time. The way she plays with all of the chess pieces (aka the men in her life) and as seen above some of the women, is downright enviable. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>King is still such an enigma here. A few glimpses here and there, but nothing concrete. You just get the feeling that he will be just as amazing a character as Søren is.<br><br>Speaking of our favourite priest. We get a far better understanding about him in this second book. Quite a few questions about his upbringing and past are addressed. Some of it is quite shocking and heartbreaking, but one thing is for sure, he truly deserves his larger than life reputation. ;D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419284987i/13026662.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Michael and Griffin. *sighs*<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m so in love with him I can’t even think straight. Which is fine since obviously I’m not straight. And neither is he.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>What a wonderful little story and all kinds of yummy too. Oh, Ms. Reisz!<br>Michael is such a precious little thing and thank god jailbait is finally legal...for the squeemish among you. ;P <br><br>Griffin is the most beautiful character. He is wild and funny and just as unappoligetic as dear Nora. <br><br>Nothing else needs to be said. Well...ok, maybe this needs to be mentioned:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There’s something wrong with your back” …<br>“There is?”<br>Griffin grinned at him. “My welts aren’t on it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And then there is the Butler of course. Never forget the Butler...he is hilarious. <br><br>Thank you for your time. On to the next one. <br><br>**<i>and the re-read continues ;D</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/454341700" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/454341700?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454341700" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18321821980710077457"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"All summer long Griffin would top her. All summer long, she would top Michael. She'd have the best of both worlds and no vanilla sex at all."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397401i/766820._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> ♦ 5 STARS ♦</b><br/><br/>Although I already loved The Siren, the first part of the Original Sinners series, but I liked this second part of the series even more!! This series is so unique, captivating and powerfully written that it easily deserves to be on <b>favorite series</b>-list. And Tiffany Reisz has easily become on of my all time favorite writers. There ju</span>
  <span id="freeText18321821980710077457" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"All summer long Griffin would top her. All summer long, she would top Michael. She'd have the best of both worlds and no vanilla sex at all."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397401i/766820._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> ♦ 5 STARS ♦</b><br><br>Although I already loved The Siren, the first part of the Original Sinners series, but I liked this second part of the series even more!! This series is so unique, captivating and powerfully written that it easily deserves to be on <b>favorite series</b>-list. And Tiffany Reisz has easily become on of my all time favorite writers. There just isn't anything out there that even resembles the original storylines of this series in the slightest. Therefore, this series is an absolute <b>MUST READ</b>. <br><br><b>
  <u>REVIEW MIGHT CONTAIN SPOILERS FOR THOSE WHO HAVEN'T THE SIREN YET</u>
</b><br><br>At the end of The Siren, Nora has made the decision to go back to Søren. She made Wesley leave her house and she hasn't heard from him in almost a year. But she's happy being back with Søren, the man who has been equally infatuated with her since she was fifteen years old, as she is with him. <br><br><b>
  <i>"My confessions begin," Father S said,"as the confessions of many men begin - with three words."<br><br>"Father forgive me?" Michael hazarded a guess. Father S sighed.<br><br>"I met Eleanor."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397401i/766821._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Søren faces the potential of being promoted to bishop. He knows there will be a lot of extra attention to his personal life and he wants to avoiding, at all costs, that anyone would find out about his relationship with Nora. So Søren decides it's best to send Nora away for the summer. That way, he can concentrate on the intrusive reporter that's determined to unravel all of his well kept secrets, without having to worry about Nora getting involved. Instead, Nora will be spending the summer months, together with <b>"The Angel" Michael</b>, in the presence of an old friend...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"And coming down the main staircase taking two steps at a time and wearing nothing but a kilt and Doc Marten boots was the lunatic laird of the Manor himself. Griffin Fiske..."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397401i/766822._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"This is going to be a long summer, isn't it?"<br>"Eight and a half inches long if you'll recall."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Griffin Fiske</b> is the enigmatic playboy and rich kid owner of the mansion Nora and Michael will be staying it. He's easygoing, funny and surprisingly caring and I liked him from the start. His fun personality was a nice and welcome distraction along the more heavy, dramatic moments throughout the story. Nora and Griffin have known each other for a long time and they have a a strong friendship.<br><br>During the summer Nora will teach Michael how to become a good submissive. Originally she's the one who will top Michael while Griffin tops her. But at the same time, Michael and Griffin start growing closer to each other too. From the moment they met, they both felt attracted to each other but neither of them was ready to admit their true feelings. As the summer progresses however, they both find it harder and harder to hide what they're feeling.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397401i/766823._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Griffin and Michael together! Although Griffin is a lot more experienced in the BDSM lifestyle than Michael, neither of them had ever been in a real relationship. They both have a lot to learn but they obviously care about each other a lot and they're both willing to make an effort for each other.<br><br>As for Nora, she finds herself often still thinking about Wesley, her former assistant, roommate and best friend. She finds herself comparing the two of them and it's obvious, the two of them could not be more different.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Winter," she finally said, "can be so beautiful and so cruel. Cruel and cold. And if you live in the presence of winter, you never have summer." Nora stepped close to him and put her nose at his cheeck. "You smell like summer. Like clean laundry hanging out in the sun. That's an amazing smell too."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Søren is like <b>winter</b>.<br>Wesley is like <b>summer</b>.<br><br>Both of them have their own special meaning to Nora. And while she's used to pain and love going hand in hand with Søren, she's starting to realize that maybe these two things don't necessarily have to go together.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397401i/766824.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Would she ever know what love without pain felt like? Did such a thing even exist?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397401i/766825._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When the summer is over, will she return to Søren, the one who has taught her everything and who has owned her heart since the moment she first met him...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Jeg elsker dig. Du er mit hjerte."<br>I love you. You are my heart.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Or will she give the lightness of summer and Wesley and a chance...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397401i/766826.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"No safe word can protect her heart..."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>

    <a title="Mo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11856352-mo"><img alt="Mo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371247812p2/11856352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/697280224?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16049178-the-angel">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Mo by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3069040-angie-loves-angst">Angie **loves angst**</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer697280224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6321576590684410592"><b>SPOILERS - do not read this if you have not read the previous books</b><br/><br/><br/>Wasn’t sure anything could TOP The Siren… I was wrong. This book blew me away. This author is fantastic. She seriously has done her homework on the Catholic Church. As I speak, listening to the Radio, somebody else is on talking about the Magdelene Launderies, the Church, Catholicism. Will you “get” this book if you are not a Catholic? Yes, I definitely think so. The author is so talented that she can transcend any faith/persuasi</span>
  <span id="freeText6321576590684410592" style="display:none"><b>SPOILERS - do not read this if you have not read the previous books</b><br><br><br>Wasn’t sure anything could TOP The Siren… I was wrong. This book blew me away. This author is fantastic. She seriously has done her homework on the Catholic Church. As I speak, listening to the Radio, somebody else is on talking about the Magdelene Launderies, the Church, Catholicism. Will you “get” this book if you are not a Catholic? Yes, I definitely think so. The author is so talented that she can transcend any faith/persuasion. <br><br>I was intrigued by SØREN in the first book. Did I like him? Not really. Did I want him? Most definitely. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Jesus, lusting after a Priest – going straight to Hell for that. <br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>We meet all the characters again and are introduced to some more. Nora, she is the best. Absolutely love her. I want to be her. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>NORA</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418108i/827646._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>GRIFFIN</b>
</blockquote><br><br>What a hoot he was …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433405i/872184.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>MICHAEL</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Michael, Michael, Michael – tortured soul ….<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298712ra/687183.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Loved their story …<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380778674i/3122241._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>“… last minute he gets nailed on a thirty year old abuse accusation. So instead of becoming bishop, he’s getting sent to wherever they send the sex offenders.”<br>“They send the sex offenders to another church full of children usually.”</b><br><br>So, so true, Suzanne. The amount of cases that have been exposed, especially in Ireland about Priests being moved from Parish to fucking Parish!<br><br>There was so much going on in this book. It seemed at the end of every chapter a new revelation was there for us to consider.<br><br>We are introduced to Suzanne, a reporter, who has demons of her own. She hates the Catholic Church and for very good reasons.<br><br><b>Some Catholics, especially the older generation, considered suicide the most dire of all sins.</b><br><br>I thinks the times are a changing in that regard. At least now they are buried in consecrated ground.<br><br>This review is probably going to be all over the place because the story was all over the place, in a totally good way. We went from NORA to SØREN to MICHAEL to GRIFFIN, a brief glimpse into the life of WES, Nora’s mother, KINGSLEY, even get to catch up with ZACH.<br><br><b>“Jesus H. Christ.” Nora groaned. “Why priests can’t keep their holy cocks inside their goddamn pants is beyond me.”</b><br><br>I know one priest who I would have no problem with taking his cock out of his pants …<br><br>As I said, I did not really like SØREN in the first book…. Yes, he was sexy, gorgeous, etc. but just could not warm to him. No problem with him in this book. His character and personality was built up very well by the author. Jesus, what a lonely life it is for a priest. Seriously the Catholic Church needs to rethink its fucking laws on “celibacy”. Before I got married, I had to do a “pre-marriage course” – cannot even remember what it was about. Probably telling us that sex was for procreation and nothing more or some sort of shite like that. Funny thing is that the course was given by a married couple and a PRIEST. What in God’s Holy Name would he know about marriage? Seriously….. it is still the same 20 or so years later. I see it in the notice board at Church – “Those of you who are getting married in the future must do a Pre-Marriage course. Please contact XXXX for details”<br><br><br><b>A celibate priest doing marriage counseling? Suzanne shook her head. What on earth could a catholic priest know about sex or marriage or romantic relationships of any kind?</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>SØREN</b>
</blockquote><br><br>SØREN in his clerical garb.<br>SØREN playing soccer (or football as I call it)<br>SØREN on a Motorcycle<br>SØREN just SØREN … no words for him!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433405i/872185._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But how could a Catholic priest be so … She couldn’t even find the right word. Attractive? Beautiful? Desirable?</b><br><br><br><b>“You called me Father comfortably, not Pastor or Reverend. And you have a distinctly Catholic look in your eyes”<br>“What Catholic look?”<br>“Guilt.”</b><br><br>Catholic guilt – does it ever leave you I wonder?<br><br>Sorry, to get back to the plot. Suzanne receives a fax with SØREN’s name on it with <i>
  <b>*conflict of interest</b>
</i> written on it…. She is intrigued. Her brother, Adam, has recently died and she has absolutely no love of the Catholic Church. SØREN’S name is being put forward as the next Bishop. Does he want the job? Not really. Does Nora want him to become Bishop. Not really. Do the people of his Parish want him to leave? Not really. Suzanne decides he needs to be investigated…. She automatically assumes that the conflict of interest is something to do with Paedophilia – is she correct? <br><br>I wonder will Suzanne feature in future stories. There is definitely an attraction between them…. If I didn’t already love him at this stage what SØREN did for Suzanne at the end of the book was beautiful..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433405i/872186.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>SØREN is a member of the Church of the Sacred Heart.<br>30 years ago you could not go into a house in Ireland without seeing a picture like this one hanging up in the kitchen – my mother still has her one over the fireplace….<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380778674i/3122242.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380778674i/3122243.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“My confession begins,” Father S said, “as the confessions of many men begin - with three words”<br><br>“Father forgive me?” Michael hazarded a guess. Father S signed.<br><br>“I met Eleanor.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433405i/872187.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>THERE WAS SO MUCH GOING ON IN THIS BOOK THAT I COULD WRITE A BLOODY THESIS ON IT SO I BETTER JUST SHUT UP AND START THE NEXT ONE …. Twists and turns at every corner. I LOVED IT!<br><br><br><b>Original Sin</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433405i/872188.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>“I’ll come back,” she promised. “I’ll always come back to you.”<br>“I know,” he said with cold, calm arrogance. <br>“If I didn’t believe that, I wouldn’t let you go.”<br>“Believe it. It’s true.” <br>She took a step back. <br>Then another. “Always.”<br><br>“Eleanor, if you have any mercy in that dark heart of yours, when you leave right now, you will walk and not run.”<br><br>“I’d never run from you, remember? But I’ll always run back.”<br><br>She didn’t crawl and she didn’t fly.<br>She ran. <br>Down the hall she ran as if the hounds of hell nipped at her heels. She ran as if God himself had ordered her to. She ran as if her life depended on it and in that moment she might have sworn that it did.<br>She didn’t know why she ran. <br>She didn’t know who or what waited for her in the White Room.<br>She only knew she had to get there as fast as she could and whoever it was, he was worth<br>running to.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433405i/872189._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I said to myself when I finished this book that I would not start the next one for a few days. I just find them very intense reading…. Not sure if I can keep my promise. I am dying to find out what happens next.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380778674i/3122245.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
