<div id="review_337655455" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/337655455" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/337655455?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer337655455" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14929501494433845450">All I can say at this late hour is "You lucky fucking bitch!"<br/><br/>Now that I've gotten some sleep... I can gather my thoughts on this one!!! What a fabulous story!!! <br/>The Angel is a continuation of the story introduced in The Siren, a glimpse into what happens next in the life of Nora Sutherlin as well as a closer look into the past lives of Nora's men, the elusive Søren, Kingsley Edge, Griffin Fiske, Wes Railey and The Angel... Michael Dimir. <br/><br/>First and foremost is Father Marcus Lennox Stearns... Søre</span>
  <span id="freeText14929501494433845450" style="display:none">All I can say at this late hour is "You lucky fucking bitch!"<br><br>Now that I've gotten some sleep... I can gather my thoughts on this one!!! What a fabulous story!!! <br>The Angel is a continuation of the story introduced in The Siren, a glimpse into what happens next in the life of Nora Sutherlin as well as a closer look into the past lives of Nora's men, the elusive Søren, Kingsley Edge, Griffin Fiske, Wes Railey and The Angel... Michael Dimir. <br><br>First and foremost is Father Marcus Lennox Stearns... Søren. The breathtakingly handsome and brilliant Catholic priest who also happens to be a sadist and The 8th Circle's lead and most feared Dominant. We get a much more in-depth look into Søren's past, and into the man himself. And oh my.... is he AMAZING!!!! He is sexy and alluring.. a sadist yes, but definitely worth the pain. He has a capacity to love that compares with no other. I have completely fallen in love with Søren!!!! I wouldn't have thought it possible... but getting to know him in this book has shed a completely different light on him for me!!!! I want more!!!!<br>Finally, I understand his love for Nora and his relationship with Kingsley. <br><br><i>
  <b>"Eleanor, will you ever learn that when I say 'I love you' I mean it?" "Eventually maybe," she said.</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>"Nora reached out and touched the wound over Søren's heart. A superficial cut, it would heal in just days. The wounds underneath, however, were old and scarified and likely would never completely heal. Scar tissue, she'd once read, was the strongest of all tissues. Maybe Søren's heart was so strong because it was so scarred."</b>
</i><br><br>I also love the way the story unfolded. Centering around an investigation, one that threatens to destroy Søren's career as a priest, and Nora's reputation, the truth seeps out slowly and surely, and from none other than the mouths of the accused. I can't remember when I last read a book where I had an OMG moment at the end of almost EVERY chapter!! <br><br>And I cannot fail to mention my latest crush... Griffin Fucking Fiske!!!!! Incredibly hot, and gregarious, it is impossible to NOT fall in love with him!!!!!! And that vision of him in that kilt....throwing Nora over his shoulder...JESUS!!!! that one's going to stay with me for a while!!! It was also wonderful watching him fall in love with Mick!! Just perfect Tiff!!!! Loved every second of it!!!!<br><br><i>
  <b>"And coming down the main spiral staircase taking two steps at a time and wearing nothing but a black kilt and Doc Marten boots was the lunatic laird of the manor himself."</b>
</i><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/meninkilts-1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379795413i/604933._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo meninkilts-1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Nora's response: <i>
  <b>"This is going to be a long summer, isn't it?"</b>
</i><br>Griffin's response: <i>
  <b>"Eight and a half inches long, if you'll recall."</b>
</i><br><br>I loved Griffin's surly British butler, and Griffin's condescending remarks to him. Great witty banter! It was frequent and fabulous... "Pope Whatadick"!!! I LOVE IT!!!<br><br>There were also many incredibly touching moments, tearful moments, moments of Nora making peace with herself and her life choices. Her explanation of love, comparing her feelings between Søren and Wes with the difference between winter and summer was quite profound. I also love how she described their smells..<br><br><i>
  <b>"Winter," she finally said, "can be beautiful and so cruel. Cruel and cold. And if you live in the presence of winter you never have summer." Nora stepped close to him and put her nose at his cheek. "You smell like summer. Like clean laundry hanging out in the sun. That's an amazing smell too."</b>
</i><br><br>All in all, I loved this book!!! No less than 5 STARS!!!!! I think Tiffany Reisz is a brilliant writer, and I will wait with bated breath for her next release....The Prince.... and we all know who that is going to be!!! SQUEEEEEEEE!!!! LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE LOVE!!!!!<br><br>Thanks Tiff for sharing your work with us!!!!!!!!<br><br><b>Nora</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/rachel_weisz02-1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1138278037" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12937608094707304867"><i>“Many waters cannot quench love, Nor will rivers overflow it. Song of Solomon 8: 7.” </i><br/><br/><b>“4.5 best ending ever stars”</b><blockquote>
  <i>And Nora didn’t walk <br/>and she didn’t crawl <br/>and she didn’t fly.<br/>She ran.</i>
</blockquote>I waited for this very moment for past few days; you can imagine my level of happiness, that I’m writing this review after 45 hours of finishing it and I still have this big fat stupid grin plastered to my face, can’t seem to stop thinking and re-thinking this epic ending!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419516610ra/13086792.gif' width='410' height='260' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Another amazing book by Tiffany Reisz, th</span>
  <span id="freeText12937608094707304867" style="display:none"><i>“Many waters cannot quench love, Nor will rivers overflow it. Song of Solomon 8: 7.” </i><br><br><b>“4.5 best ending ever stars”</b><blockquote>
  <i>And Nora didn’t walk <br>and she didn’t crawl <br>and she didn’t fly.<br>She ran.</i>
</blockquote>I waited for this very moment for past few days; you can imagine my level of happiness, that I’m writing this review after 45 hours of finishing it and I still have this big fat stupid grin plastered to my face, can’t seem to stop thinking and re-thinking this epic ending!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419516610ra/13086792.gif" width="410" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Another amazing book by Tiffany Reisz, this woman officially rocked my world! Beautiful young love, complicated characters, gut-wrenching revelations, incomplete romance-This story by far surpasses any stories I’ve read about love, life, friendship and sacrifice. <br><br>The characters TR creates are with absolute perfection and very realistic, you just wish to be like them, better yet to be with them. In any other world this story would be a scandalized tale of sinners, but we love them unconditionally and hope these damaged souls find their very own <i>Angel</i><br><br><b>Kingsley</b><blockquote>
  <i> “Who is Kingsley? Kingsley Edge, <br>the King of Kink in New York City. <br>Half-French, all pervert.” </i>
</blockquote>My favorite sexy Frenchman, he was enigmatic and distant but his love and commitment was simply heart touching! I seriously hope his true love comes back to him.<br><br><b>Griffin</b><blockquote>
  <i> “I’m sexual-harassment lawsuit waiting to happen.”</i>
</blockquote>Griffin….<i>*sighs*</i> smart, sexy, amazing, funny, charming and AWESOME!! Loved his snarky remarks specially one’s about the pope <i>*winks*</i><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “You know I don't mind sloppy seconds. <br>And knowing Pope Whatadick, <br>he probably blesses his cum before he blows it”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> I wish there was lot more to Griffin and his butler’s banters! It was FUCKING HILARIOUS!!!<br><br><i> “Master Griffin, I would marry my own mother for the excuse to stab <br>my eyes out with her brooches than to see anything under your kilt,” <br>"Thank you, Alfred," Griffin said, taking the supplies.</i><br><br><b>♥Michael &amp; Griffin♥</b><blockquote>
  <i> “I want Griffin.”<br>“I want Griffin so much it hurts. I love him, Nora.” </i>
</blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419516610ra/13086793.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Most cutest sweetest adorable couple among the kinksters! <br><br><b>
  <i> “…Michael is absolutely, completely, ridiculously beautiful.” <br>“Nora...” Griffin said in a distressed voice. “I Think I’m in love.” </i>
</b><br><br>I’m in love with these two! Everything about them, their innocence, bonding, affection, sexual tension and mostly their love was to die for! This being my first M/M romance, I loved the hell out of them♥ Griffin was initially introduced as a playboy ex-drug addict dom who has never been in a real relationship but when he first lays his eyes on Michael he knew he wanted him so badly. Michael just like his name is a beautiful Angel, he learns to accept his desire and comes out of his shell to embrace the love he feels for Griffin.<br><br>Oh boy! Never knew guy on guy action could be so damn HAWT!! Everything about them is perfect, did I say how much I love them?! I’m in a sugar rush with all their sweetness! <br><br><b>Søren</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/535052.gif" width="360" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I...ummm...I think...I Kinda...umm.. Love him. I Love Søren. There...I said it!!! It’s a Christmas miracle! Never knew I will stop hating him let alone adore him. Last 10% of the story really changed my mind towards him. I get why everyone loves him- he’s doesn’t mind Nora’s infidelity since he knows that he owns her and that she will ALWAYS comes back to him no matter how many sexual partners she had who worships the ground she walks on. That’s the power of his love, he may be a sadist but he’ll kill anyone who ever hurt her without her consent. Not only he’s kind, generous and super smart but dude does intimidate me at times!<br><br><b>Nora</b><br><br><i>Dear Nora,<blockquote>Have you lost your fucking mind?!</blockquote>I spent four days hating Soren, getting intimated by him all the time because that’s how you painted him bitch! Will you for love of the god make up your mind about your true feelings! Throughout Siren all I heard was Søren is dangerous, he’s a sadist, he hits you, humiliated you and that you left him for good blah blah blah… and you go running to him because that’s where you thought you belonged, almost stomping my heart in that process. I was so sick worried what how badly he’s going to hurt you and here the very first page I see you enjoying his holy cock inside you! <br><br>It’s a year since you are back with the pope and guess what I’m hearing? Søren is a devoted lover, amazing person, I would spend my eternity with him! <b> I will die in my collar.”</b> ooh! This is my favorite one <b>“Søren’s the best man on the face of the earth,”</b> now that sounds familiar, wait! I know where I heard that! You almost said the same thing about Wes</i>. <br><br>You are still awesome minus being emotionally stupid! Let me give you a piece of advice- <b>KEEP YOUR SHIT TOGETHER</b> Nora, I swear if you hurt my baby boy again... <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419516610i/13086794._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Rating Clarification</b>: only reason I couldn’t give perfect 5 stars because IMO Søren was introduced as different person here. I remember complaining about not knowing him in Siren but there he was pictured as a evil sadist and even with few flashbacks I saw him beating the shit out of her or being a manipulative bastard but here I didn’t see any mean streaks to him even his bloodplay felt romantic! No pain no belts no whips no slaps no humiliation but a perfect lover!<br>I’m glad I saw the sane side of Soren, understood his love, loyalty and kindness but I felt I was misguided! <br><br><i>Buddy read with insanely awesome Eda!♥ Sorry to torture you which all the teasers, but babe you really are a evil genius when it comes to the story-line *winks* love reading with you...muahhh!!</i><br></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/443796742" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/443796742?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE who wants epic reads!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=mind-fuckery">mind-fuckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443796742" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2595772552670626993"><b>5++++ Amazing Stars!<br/><br/><br/><i>Many waters cannot quench love, nor will rivers overflow it. </i></b><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/697E905B-6C2A-4DC8-B944-CC09026EBCBC_zpspfcyxd62.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418826127i/12915241._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 697E905B-6C2A-4DC8-B944-CC09026EBCBC_zpspfcyxd62.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>There aren't many series out there where I have much desire to re-read them. I mean, I know the story and how it ends. What's really to gain? What did I gain rereading <b>The Angel?</b> An even deeper, profound respect for this author. I recently tried to explain <i>the TOS phenomenon </i> to a friend and I compared it to an episode of "Friends," where there's not one or two MCs, but a conglomerate of characters, all adding t</span>
  <span id="freeText2595772552670626993" style="display:none"><b>5++++ Amazing Stars!<br><br><br><i>Many waters cannot quench love, nor will rivers overflow it. </i></b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/697E905B-6C2A-4DC8-B944-CC09026EBCBC_zpspfcyxd62.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418826127i/12915241._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 697E905B-6C2A-4DC8-B944-CC09026EBCBC_zpspfcyxd62.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>There aren't many series out there where I have much desire to re-read them. I mean, I know the story and how it ends. What's really to gain? What did I gain rereading <b>The Angel?</b> An even deeper, profound respect for this author. I recently tried to explain <i>the TOS phenomenon </i> to a friend and I compared it to an episode of "Friends," where there's not one or two MCs, but a conglomerate of characters, all adding their piece to the puzzle, making it perfectly balanced in the end. Typically, books with several characters tend to muck the story for me, almost confusing me, but Ms. Reisz carries her readers through their lives seamlessly. Each book moving us forward, all the while, giving us background at the same time. Happiness, sadness, pain, suffering, victory but never defeat. <br><br>The biggest highlight in this book for me.....drum roll please.<br><br><b>GRIFFIN! </b>(and his antics with his butler- epic)<br><br><i>Jamison appeared in the doorway with a cooler.<br>"Thank you, Alfred," Griffin said, taking the supplies. "There's a thousand dollars in the cookie jar. Go buy yourself something pretty."<br>"I will purchase a firearm and shoot you with it," Griffin's butler said, bowing elegantly. "Master Griffin."<br>He left the room. <br><br><br>-or-<br><br><br>“Alfred, I need ice and that vitamin K goop. To the nursery. Stat."<br>"I loathe you, Master Griffin," came a British accent over the intercom.<br>"Thanks, Alfred," Griffin answered and came back to the bed.<br>"Is your butler's name really Alfred?"<br>"No. It's Jamison, I think. Can't remember. I changed it to Alfred years ago. My first crush on a dude was Batman.</i><br><br><br>Sweet Jesus, I forgot how much I loved Griffin until I reread this book! OMG the guy is so stinking endearingly cute. A filthy rich trust-fund kid, he grabbed my attention from the minute he waltzed down his mansion stairs in a Scottish kilt and Doc Maartens. Definitely a site to behold, I'm sure. But watching this Dom/man-whore fall head over heels for the stunningly beautiful <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Michael <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was the highlight for me. Consummating that relationship even more so!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/M%20and%20M/89D0B368-063E-4499-8A05-7431C9EF0BA4_zpszbas3qno.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418866281ra/12926596.gif" alt=" photo 89D0B368-063E-4499-8A05-7431C9EF0BA4_zpszbas3qno.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Each character has their flaws, their crosses to bear, yet their combined bond and support for each other is unbreakable. God help anyone who messes with one "of them."<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/8D804C13-BBFE-42B6-961B-41D3A45150FA_zpsloowjy78.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418826127i/12915242._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8D804C13-BBFE-42B6-961B-41D3A45150FA_zpsloowjy78.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>When I first read this series a couple years ago, this was my least favorite book...relatively speaking since all four of them I rated five stars. Since then, I've delved into more MM reads and I found this book a lot more <i>enjoyable. </i><br><br><br>I feel like reviewing any Original Sinners book is futal since the plot thickens with each book and any details are serious spoilers. Just know, there's a character for everyone to love in TOS. Ya like an intimidating, omnipresent, yet reserved persona in a hero? A sarcastic, smooth talking Frenchmen? A tough, snarky heroine? A sweet, virginal, beautiful yet scarred victim? A crazy, sarcastic, rich Bisexual Dom? You name it, TOS has it!<br><br>Moving on to my (third) read of The Prince (my FAVE). God, I'm such a Frenchman whore...<br><br><br>❤️<i>Buddy re-read with Jasmine</i>❤️</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2595772552670626993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer372272862" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2934298126216459519">Preliminary review-This book is amazing. Just amazing. Tiffany Reisz is so damn smart. She makes you think. She makes you feel. She makes you question yourself and your beliefs. She's not afraid of the darknessthat resides in a character's soul and she's not afraid drag you along with her into that darkness.. Nothing is taboo with her, and she makes you feel like you should reconsider what you consider taboo. All of her characters are relatable. All are human, flawed and beautiful.<br/><br/>Søren, in the </span>
  <span id="freeText2934298126216459519" style="display:none">Preliminary review-This book is amazing. Just amazing. Tiffany Reisz is so damn smart. She makes you think. She makes you feel. She makes you question yourself and your beliefs. She's not afraid of the darknessthat resides in a character's soul and she's not afraid drag you along with her into that darkness.. Nothing is taboo with her, and she makes you feel like you should reconsider what you consider taboo. All of her characters are relatable. All are human, flawed and beautiful.<br /><br />Søren, in the Siren, was not my favorite character. I like him much more now. I understand him better. We get to see the complexity of all of these wonderful characters. The addition of Michael is a beautiful one. There's a lot of character growth and definitely more sex. Reisz's characters have layers upon layers that are rarely seen in literature. She's a gifted writer. No one can write a Switch like Ms. Reisz, no one.<br /><br />If you like BDSM, this series cannot be missed. It will be a classic one day. Of this, I'm sure.<br /><br />As reviewed for Read Our Lips Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.readourlipsblog.blogspot.mx/2012/10/nsfw-review-angel-original-sinners-2-by.html#more">http://www.readourlipsblog.blogspot.m...</a><br /><br />The Angel by Tiffany Reisz: Blew. Me. Away.  It's the kind of read you wish wouldn’t end with twists and turns you'd never anticipate, evoking emotions you never expected.  <br /><br />The Angel picks up a year later after the ending of The Siren. Nora is back together with Søren.  We get to see some play scenes between the two of them, which we fans have been waiting to see for so long.  Those two live up to the hype, let me tell you.  And finally!  We get to see some love and tenderness between these two!  Tiffany Reisz (TR or Mistress Tiff) made us wait a long time for that! But it was definitely worth the wait.<br /><br />To protect everyone involved from a work issue that's dogging Søren, he sends Nora away and has her take Michael (the White Room Virgin from The Siren) with her to begin his training as a submissive.  Nora decides to go to upstate New York and visit Griffin.  We all remember Griffin from The Siren, right?  Sexy Dom with great muscles, hair, and smile?  Yum.  So it's just the three of them in Griffin's big house for the period of exile.<br /><br />With Griffin topping Nora, who's topping Michael, this equals to so much sexiness, it makes you squirm in the best possible sense. The three of them together and all their debauchery for a summer were some of my favorite scenes.  At one point, Griffin is wearing a kilt and nothing else.  Be still my heart!<br /><br />Add to the landscape, Suzanne, a reporter investigating Søren.  Suzanne has demons of her own – namely a brother who committed suicide, the biggest triggering factor having been molested by a priest in childhood.  Her faith is in question.  Suzanne has a very primal attraction to Søren.  She wants him.  With Nora gone for the Summer, Søren is short a play partner...<br /><br />Suzanne gets to go a bit down the rabbit hole, but all under the guiding hand of Søren and of course Kingsley the Omnipotent.  Suzanne's investigating an anonymous tip she received about Søren, and through her digging we learn about Søren's beginnings.  I have to say, I like Søren a LOT more in this book, than I did in The Siren. <br /><br />We get to see some of the bricks of his foundation and to say it's shocking is an understatement.   This is where TR shines.  She can take a book that is so enjoyable and sexy and bring an abysmal darkness into it.  All the while, she protects you from the deep despair that would normally accompany reading such a harsh subject matter.  Usually, it would be hard for me to move to a lighter scene after such darkness is exposed, but TR is just so good at weaving the human conditions which plagues us all.  Her writing makes you feel protected, I think much in the way Søren's subjects feel protected by him.  You may take the fall, but she'll give you a soft place to land.  I have no idea how she does it.  But it's one of the things that has always made her one of my favorite authors.<br /><br />Notably missing is Wesley, but not for long.  I'm not going to spoil you on this one.  But just so you know,  I desperately covet Wes' combs.<br /><br />The Angel is not to be missed.  TR is like one of those World Record setting Domino Toppling Players.  You know – the ones who set up tens of thousands of dominoes; up stairs, around corners, then back down stairs, and it all starts with one. . . little . . . push. The Angel is brilliantly woven, with wonderfully sweet moments as well as incredibly disturbing revelations.  While on this journey, I have no idea where TR’s taking me, but I love the hell outta the trip!  I have the feeling we've only just begun our Original Sinners journey and I eagerly await the next installment - The Prince.<br /><br /><br /><br /> <br /><br />What I liked about The Angel: <br /><br />Reunion. I finally get the reunion between Søren and Nora that I wanted in The Siren.  Tenderness included.<br />Søren. I have now fallen prey to Søren's hotness.<br />Back story. We get more of Søren and Nora's back story. Together and Separate. Hold onto your hats!<br />Griffin. I adore him. Sexiness aside, his playful nature and huge heart would have even the coldest reader swooning.  He is a natural Dom, protective to the Nth degree and a smart-ass to boot.  Love, love, love Griffin!<br />Tattoo time and everything that went with it.  Everyone should get their tats from a purple-haired, Scottish chick named Spike.<br />Healing. Søren's assistance in helping Suzanne heal.<br />Wesley's talk with Søren. Boy's got cajones. <br />Nora's big heart. She may be a switch, but she's also a nurturer.<br />Michael, Nora's Angel. I love his sweetness, his bravery, his capacity for love.  His submission is beautiful.  He's very special and TR makes sure we know it.<br />The ending.  Here's how I feel about the ending-*twirly, whirly-gig, Lucy from Peanuts dance, ending in beautiful ballet on tip-toe, (I took tap and jazz, I don't know the names for these, sorry!) and Plié.*<br /><br /><br />What I didn't like about The Angel :<br /><br />*crickets*<br />Nada </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5780313813468506090"><b>5 +++ Controversial, Scorching, Addictive Stars!! It blew me away and I’m still recovering!!</b><br/><br/><i>“Fetishes…they’re the pet you feed or the beast that eats you.” <br/>We’ll feed your beast until it’s tamed.”</i>-Nora Sutherlin<br/><br/>Check your morals and beliefs at the first page, because this book will have you looking deep inside yourself and leave you contemplating about everything you’ve read. If the unconventional is the solution in healing persons, who might otherwise not fare well with so-called accepted pract</span>
  <span id="freeText5780313813468506090" style="display:none"><b>5 +++ Controversial, Scorching, Addictive Stars!! It blew me away and I’m still recovering!!</b><br /><br /><i>“Fetishes…they’re the pet you feed or the beast that eats you.” <br />We’ll feed your beast until it’s tamed.”</i>-Nora Sutherlin<br /><br />Check your morals and beliefs at the first page, because this book will have you looking deep inside yourself and leave you contemplating about everything you’ve read. If the unconventional is the solution in healing persons, who might otherwise not fare well with so-called accepted practices, what can it hurt, when they are hurting so much already?!?! Their normal might not be yours, but if it permits them to feel whole and ultimately endure, who are we to judge? If it hurts no one other than themselves, but that hurt has the power to heal, and they give themselves to someone unconditionally, one who can give them what them so desire…who are we to criticize?<br /><br />I can't remember when a book turned my world upside down, had my heart in my throat, gave my brain a workout...oh wait…yes I can…that would have been <i>The Siren</i>!! Somehow though, this one knocked me for a bigger loop, sucked the life out of me! <i>The Angel</i> topped <i>The Siren</i> from the bottom. The second book had even more control and command over me than the first one did! I don’t even know if that makes any sense. <br /><br />This book is like a Jack-in-the-Box…page, page, page…shocker…page, page, page…shocker, over and over. You crank the handle, then you wait with baited breath for the next revelation…you’re stunned, at times repulsed, horrified, but you have to continue reading. The story, the characters, their circumstances, how they deal and overcome, is fascinating, debatable and highly addictive!<br /><br />The book is very erotic and some of that eroticism is questionable, especially when it comes to Michael. I’m on the fence about this with him, because of his age, and what he does, or, what is done to him. However, his alternative solution, should he not be allowed to do what he desires and what he<b> NEEDS</b>, would bring about the end of him, and I would rather he be allowed to live his “normal”, whether we agree with it or not. <br /><br />Yes, there is blood play in this book and it didn’t appall me as much as I thought it would. It seemed incredibly painful, yet unbelievably intimate. I can’t believe I just said that! But, that’s how I feel. I’m just fascinated by this whole world and wouldn’t mind spending some time in this alternate universe. Does that make me a freak or weirdo (Michael’s words not mine)?? Maybe, I can't deny that I'm curious. <br /> <br />Soren is an imposing, arrogant, extraordinary presence! I was drawn to him once again, he holds all the power, but uses it very carefully. He’s also understanding and an honorable man. Yes, honorable, and extremely protective, giving and loving!! I find him to be one of the most intriguing and appealing characters I’ve ever read about. <br /><br />Nora was Nora. Funny, sassy, flies by the seat of her pants and wants nothing more than to do right by Michael; albeit it will have you raising your eyebrows, as does her relationship with Griffin. They use each other sexually, like they’re having tea and cookies; it’s weird, but kind of funny! Griffin stole my heart in this book for all he is and what he does…I love him and have a new found respect for him!! Oh my, Kingsley, do tell, what goes through that mind of yours. I can’t wait to experience more of him. Wow, just thinking of what’s to come, has me drenched!! Wesley, I won’t say much about him…only that he’s delicious and his story is waiting to be told, let’s just leave it at that. <br /><br />Tiffany Reisz wrote a <b>FANTASTIC</b>, well-written, well-thought out book. It is sensual, passionate, humorous, heart-wrenching, but also has some unbelievably heart-warming moments. It messes with your mind, what you want to detest, abhor, and despise…starts to make sense. The dialogue is amazing and deliciously witty!! Just a warning… this read is not for everyone, and you have to have an open mind, open heart and understand the book for what it is. If you can deal with some questionable issues, no correction, lots of questionable issues, then I HIGHLY recommend it, and then go ahead and become immersed, and lost in the intensity of Tiffany Reisz’s writing. It will mess with your psyche, play with your emotions and when you come out the other side of it, you won’t know which end is up!! One of the best, if not the best book I’ve read this year. Pretty amazing when <i>The Siren</i> held that spot until <i>The Angel</i> edged it out with its awesomeness! <br /><br />I’m torn over the ending and my heart is heavy, but I truly believe that, (huge)<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ as much as I love Wesley, I believe in my heart that he is in love with the idea of Nora and Nora is in love with the idea of normal, but Soren’s love for her is bone deep and what he offers, albeit unconventional, it’s what she needs! “Are you going to stay with the one who loves you, or are you going to run to the one you love”-<i>The One You Love</i> by Glenn Frey.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It remains to be seen. <br /><br />This amazing song, <i>I'm not Jesus</i>, is dedicated to all the Adams in the world, (huge)<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and for Michael, Soren and Elizabeth who were hurt so bad at the hands of their fathers <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>…your pain and suffering is <b>unforgiveable!!</b><br /><br /><i>I’m not Jesus</i> by Apocalyptica featuring Corey Taylor<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PMLsF8ajI6U">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PMLsF8...</a><br /><br /><i>Dirty little secret, <br />Dirty little lies. <br />Say your prayers and comb your hair, <br />Save your soul tonight. <br /><br />Drift among the faithful, <br />Bury your desires. <br />Aberrations fill your head, <br />You need a place to hide <br />And I am... <br /><br />Do you remember me? <br />And the kid I used to be? <br />Do you remember me? <br /><br />When your world's come crashing down <br />I want to relive. <br />(Your god ain't looking down on me!) <br /><br />I'm not Jesus, <br />Jesus wasn't there! <br /><br />You confess it all away, <br />But it's only shit to me <br />(Your god ain't looking down on me!) <br /><br />I'm not Jesus, <br />I will not forgive! <br /><br />No I won't! <br />No I won't. <br /><br />I thought you were a good man, <br />I thought you talked to god. <br />You hippocratic, messianic, <br />And child abusing-turned-satanic. <br /><br />Do you remember me? <br />Do you remember me? <br />And the kid I used to be? <br />Do you remember? <br />Do you remember? <br /><br />When your own world comes undone, <br />Let me be the one to say: <br />(Your god ain't looking down on me!) <br /><br />"I'm not Jesus, <br />You can't run away!" <br /><br />And the innocence you spoiled <br />Found a way to live. <br />(Your god ain't looking down on me!) <br /><br />I'm not Jesus <br />I will not forgive! <br /><br />I'm not Jesus, <br />I will not, <br />I'm not Jesus, <br />I will not forgive! <br /><br />Oh, I will not forgive, <br />No, I will not forgive!</i><br /><br /><i>*ARC kindly provided by HarlequinMIRA via NetGalley*</i><br /><br />My apologies for this lengthy review, but I think it says something about the book! <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5780313813468506090" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer449242854" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9507809828072434107"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Fetishes...they're the pet the pet that you feed or the beast that eats you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764759.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>To say that I loved this book would probably be an understatement. I fucking loved it! This series is captivating, dark, erotic, and completely addictive.<br/><br/>The Angel picks up 13 months where The Siren ended. After Nora's devastating decision with Wesley, she is now with Soren. The Angel gives us something that we didn't get much of in the previous book, some of Soren's history. Although he is still a very dar</span>
  <span id="freeText9507809828072434107" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Fetishes...they're the pet the pet that you feed or the beast that eats you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764759.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>To say that I loved this book would probably be an understatement. I fucking loved it! This series is captivating, dark, erotic, and completely addictive.<br><br>The Angel picks up 13 months where The Siren ended. After Nora's devastating decision with Wesley, she is now with Soren. The Angel gives us something that we didn't get much of in the previous book, some of Soren's history. Although he is still a very dark character, and still scares me a bit, particularly with his <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[hard core sadism <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, I am starting to warm up to him more. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396624ra/764760.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Soren finds out that he is being considered as the possible replacement for the bishop and someone has broken into Kingsley's office and stole Nora's file, he knows the best thing for everyone is to send Nora away for a little while. The last thing they need is a closer look at their relationship, so he decides to send Nora away together with Michael to stay at the house of Griffin Fiske for the summer.<br><br>Michael, although now slightly older at 17, is still having a hard time dealing with the repercussions of his family finding out about his 'kinks'. Getting away from the brutality of his father and the lack of attention from his mother is exactly what he wants right now. Particularly for the chance to be 'trained' by the infamous Mistress Nora.<br><br>When he comes face to face with the gorgeous, tatted, and hillariously out-spoken Griffin, he is confused by his reaction to the man. Before long, Michael realizes that he is attracted to him and begins to want things he never before wanted.<br><br>Griffin was one of my favorite parts of this book. Besides him being sexy as hell, with tats and a Ducati, he has a wicked sense of humor.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Alfred, I need ice and that vitamin K goop. Stat."<br>Michael heard the crackle of static.<br>"I loathe you, Master Griffin," came a British accent over the intercom.<br>"Thanks, Alfred."<br>"Is your butler's name really Alfred?"<br>"No, it's Jamison, I think. Can't remember. I changed it to Alfred years ago. My first crush on a dude was batman."</b>
</blockquote><br>I loved the way that Griffin was with Michael. While he comes off as care-free and sarcastic, he was so caring and sweet when it came to Michael. Not to say that the steam was missing. Hell no! When they finally got together...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396624ra/764761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Their relationship is developing throughout the whole book, and it was my favorite part of The Angel.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764762.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> ***********************<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Tell me, have you ever had sex in the back of a Rolls Royce?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797101i/627231._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Kingsley is pretty much the same mystery that he was in The Siren, though we do get to find out a bit more about his relationship with Soren.<br> ************************<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Eleanor, if you have any mercy in that dark heart of yours, when you leave me right now, you will walk and not run."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764763._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>After receiving an anonymous tip that there might be a conflict of interest in his consideration for bishop, a reporter begins to investigate the enigma that is Soren. Through the investigation we get to find out Soren's dark history. Finding out what we did, it really helps put many things in perspective, though it was devastating.<br><br> ************************<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Love is the open wound that you hope never heals.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764764._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nora is still struggling with her decision of leaving Wesley. Even though Soren own her heart, she loves Wesley and can't seem to let him go.<br><blockquote>
  <b>Life with Soren was paradise, a dark, dangerous paradise but still, a perfect naked Eden.<br>"Almost perfect," she whispered to no one.</b>
</blockquote><br>While Soren fulfills the dark edges, there is still a part of her that knows Wesley has something else to offer, something that Soren will never be able to.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Winter, can be so beautiful and so cruel. Cruel and cold. And if you live in the presence of winter you never have summer." Nora stepped close to him and put her nose at his cheek. "You smell like summer. Like clean laundry hanging out in the sun. That's an amazing smell too."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br> ****************************<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764765.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Even though it has been 13 long months since he has last seen Nora, Wesley still struggles to move on and forget his love for her. He is the light to the dark that is Kingsley and Soren and the rest of Nora's world. He is so pure in his feelings, and ferocious in his love for her.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"No, she and I never had sex. That's true. But we had love, real love that didn't take anything out of us, that didn't bruise us or break us. I loved her without hurting her. You asked me if I, a virgin, could teach her what sex should be? No, of course ot. Hell no. But at least I can teach her what love should be like. And she knows it too.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764766.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> To W.R. Many waters.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>While there were many revelations, and questions that were answered, I still was left with as many questions as I received answers. I cannot wait to find out more about the mysterious Kingsley, and to see where the next book takes Nora and her relationship with Soren and Wes.<br><br><b>5 Completely Enthralling and Compelling Stars</b><br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer740093161" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5792167211266955209"><u>EDIT 12/28/13 from the Mistress herself:</u> "Also in 2014, the first four books of The Original Sinners are being released with new covers with bonus short stories at the end. You'll finally be able to own "Gauze," "Griffin in Wonderland," "Midnight Mass," and "A Beautiful Thing" in print."<br/><br/><b> 10+++++ Stars!!!!! Love this book even more than the first!</b><br/><br/>Wow. Just wow. I <b>
  <i>finally</i>
</b> understand now. Why so many love Søren. How the chain of events are connected. How all these <i>characters</i> are connected. This</span>
  <span id="freeText5792167211266955209" style="display:none"><u>EDIT 12/28/13 from the Mistress herself:</u> "Also in 2014, the first four books of The Original Sinners are being released with new covers with bonus short stories at the end. You'll finally be able to own "Gauze," "Griffin in Wonderland," "Midnight Mass," and "A Beautiful Thing" in print."<br /><br /><b> 10+++++ Stars!!!!! Love this book even more than the first!</b><br /><br />Wow. Just wow. I <b>
  <i>finally</i>
</b> understand now. Why so many love Søren. How the chain of events are connected. How all these <i>characters</i> are connected. This book....just WOW. There are <b>
  <i>truly</i>
</b> no words to describe just how mindblowing, sensational, EPIC, this book is. It is one of a kind and in its own class. To write a full-length review glorifying certain parts of the book would tarnish the perfection of the story, and for each positive brought forward, there will always be something <b>
  <i>more</i>
</b>, something <b>
  <i>deeper</i>
</b>, something <b>
  <i>unexplainable</i>
</b>, something <b>
  <i>unreachable</i>
</b>, that this review cannot possibly cover. <br /><br />I am in shock.<br /><br />I am in awe.<br /><br />I am in pain.<br /><br />I am in lust.<br /><br />I am in love.<br /><br />I am in awe.<br /><br />I am <i>
  <b>in awe.</b>
</i><br /><br />Beauty. Pain. Darkness. Light. Flaw. <b>
  <i>Perfection</i>
</b>.<br /><br />Well-done doesn't even begin to describe your marvelous writing talents Tiffany Reisz. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5792167211266955209" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1737438697" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1737438697" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1737438697?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saint Monique" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saint Monique" href="/user/show/40572117-saint-monique">Saint Monique</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780263905779" href="/book/show/16082983-the-angel">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40572117-saint-monique?shelf=omg-i-am-in-love-with-this-book">omg-i-am-in-love-with-this-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40572117-saint-monique?shelf=punish-me-with-pleasure">punish-me-with-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40572117-saint-monique?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1737438697" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7140557041136560478"><b>5 <i>'Wings'</i> stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“Love is an open wound that you hope never heals.”</b>
</blockquote><br/>First read: 9 Nov 2016 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/>Re-read: 14 Nov 2019 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/><br/>Re-reading The Angel felt like Heaven! Seriously, this series is my all-time favorite and reading it for the second time, I'm loving it even more. Should I now say it's my double favorite? <i>*grinning*</i> Anyway, my review might be slightly spoilerish (I get carried away when I am over-excited) so read at your own risk. And of course, be prepared for fangirling and a lot of swoon</span>
  <span id="freeText7140557041136560478" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>'Wings'</i> stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Love is an open wound that you hope never heals.”</b>
</blockquote><br>First read: 9 Nov 2016 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br>Re-read: 14 Nov 2019 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br><br>Re-reading The Angel felt like Heaven! Seriously, this series is my all-time favorite and reading it for the second time, I'm loving it even more. Should I now say it's my double favorite? <i>*grinning*</i> Anyway, my review might be slightly spoilerish (I get carried away when I am over-excited) so read at your own risk. And of course, be prepared for fangirling and a lot of swooning.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1572983085i/28406912._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Father S had met his eyes and Michael saw the hint of a smile in them, a secret smile and the passing shadow of a green-eyed girl who could make any man lose his religion.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>We get Michael's POV in this book <i>*happy dance*</i> I can't tell you how much I adore this Angel. The most precious character ever. And kinky as hell. Don't let his innocence fool you. He's junior kinkster indeed. I love the easy banter between him and Nora and how he's not afraid to be himself around her. And how Søren is more father to him than Michael's real father ever was.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>A good morning so far—she’d been fucked by her favorite man, hugged by her favorite boy and silently adored by her favorite angel.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Nora and Søren are happily back together and all is well in Paradies... Well, except not everything. There's always a snake, right? Troubles are brewing, so Søren sends Nora and Michael to Griffin. And OMG Griff is so gorgeous. I adore him too!<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>And coming down the main spiral staircase taking two steps at a time and wearing nothing but a black kilt and Doc Marten boots was the lunatic laird of the manor himself.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Yeah, that's Griffin. One-quarter Scottish and all crazy. And also the most spoiled trust fund baby ever. But I love how he genuinely cares about people around him. He's all humor and party on the outside but he can be so sweet and caring too. And his 69 jokes are pure gold. I'm so in love or in lust or whatever.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Number two—Michael is absolutely, completely, ridiculously beautiful.”<br>“Nora…” Griffin said in a distressed voice. “I think I’m in love.”<br>“You’re in heat, Griff. Big difference. Oh, and number three…Søren says you can’t fuck him.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Can I get all swoony again? Griffin and Michael together! They are the most adorable, precious couple. I just love them so much. They are perfect for each other. How Griff is making Michael feel more confident about himself and how Griffin became a better person for Michael. And wings tattoos <i>*le sigh*</i><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Gorgeous, Mick. They’re gorgeous.” Griffin squeezed Michael’s fingers. “Just like you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>***********************************<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I want to own you,” Griffin whispered into Michael’s ear. Michael smiled, and for the first time in his life knew exactly what to say and how to say it. “You already do.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Nora is still pinning after Wes. <i>*roll eyes*</i> I never truly understood their relationship. They are so ill-suited for each other and they are the only ones who doesn't see that. I have a feeling Nora never really thought through what she would have to give up to be with Wes. <br><br>In the meantime, Søren is dealing with a noisy reporter who is digging into his past and trying to expose his secrets. I have a feeling he had a time of his life playing cat and mouse with that annoying woman. She really had no idea what has she gotten herself into. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“It was Christ’s way to welcome sinners and tax collectors and other nefarious characters into His company and His Kingdom. On His especially compassionate and generous days, he would even speak to reporters.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>And I finally got more Kingsley in this book! Still not enough but at least I know what is waiting for me in the following books. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Nora grinned. Who was Kingsley? Kingsley Edge, the King of Kink in New York City. Half-French, all pervert.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>***********************************<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>He looked like a man who’d seen so much blood he had the Grim Reaper on speed dial.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>And we heard the most famous question of the series for the first time.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Have you ever had sex in the back of a Rolls Royce?”</blockquote>
</b><br>Yes, it's this series' fault for my obsession with Rolls Royces.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“God, they were sexy as hell, weren’t they?”<br>“Seriously,” Michael agreed as he looked over Nora’s shoulder at the black-and-white photograph. In the picture, he saw an eighteen-year-old Father S sitting casually in an armchair in a dark suit, tidy and pin neat. At his feet sat another boy, only a year younger, with longer dark hair and his Catholic school uniform artfully rumpled with the jacket abandoned, the tie loose and the collar open.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>I'm so ready for teenage Søren and Kingsley in the next book.<br><br><i>B(R)R ménage à cinq with my Sinner Ladies <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/52957386-melanie-a" rel="nofollow noopener">Melanie</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58429822-ursy" rel="nofollow noopener">Ursy</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14379473-leila" rel="nofollow noopener">Leila</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/66575688-whitney" rel="nofollow noopener">Whitney</a></i> 😇😇😇😇😇</span>
  <a data-text-id="7140557041136560478" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer7095741404259031463"><b>Review contains spoilers for The Siren</b><br/><br/><br/><b>5 Sinning Stars</b><br/><br/><i>The Angel</i> begins about a year after Nora returns to Soren. Their year back together has been perfect, but problems arise when Soren is being vetted to become Bishop. Soren concerned about people discovering his relationship with Nora determines its necessary to send her away. Michael is 17 now and in need of training so its the perfect opportunity for them to get away together and work on his training. So where should these two go….enter Griff</span>
  <span id="freeText7095741404259031463" style="display:none"><b>Review contains spoilers for The Siren</b><br><br><br><b>5 Sinning Stars</b><br><br><i>The Angel</i> begins about a year after Nora returns to Soren. Their year back together has been perfect, but problems arise when Soren is being vetted to become Bishop. Soren concerned about people discovering his relationship with Nora determines its necessary to send her away. Michael is 17 now and in need of training so its the perfect opportunity for them to get away together and work on his training. So where should these two go….enter Griffin.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383427871ra/6553743.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Since his attempted suicide his parents have treated Michael horribly. He doesn’t belong anywhere and is unsure of himself. While at Griffin’s Michael learns more about who he is and what he wants. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402453310i/9939660.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am in complete shock after finishing this book. Why you ask…well, I am in awe of Tiffany’s writing and story telling. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404388395ra/10232213.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I have no clue how she is capable of putting all this together where there is no down time in the book, and I am dying to turn the page to learn more. Its so impressive how every little details works together to mean something. <br><br>This series is like nothing I have ever read. There is no “filler” in her stories and they have completely consumed me, to the point I think about the characters in real life. This story is not just Nora and Soren, or Nora and King, or Nora and Michael…all of the characters are equally important to me which is so odd when we are used to reading books with two or three main characters. <br><br>I think everyone with an <i>open mind</i> should read this series, there is nothing to compare it to its in a league of its own. So excited to be moving on to The Prince!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404359706ra/10229907.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_348220987" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/348220987" />
    <a title="Rhonda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3078175-rhonda"><img alt="Rhonda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1391830542p2/3078175.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/348220987?book_show_action=true">Jun 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rhonda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rhonda" href="/user/show/3078175-rhonda">Rhonda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3078175-rhonda?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer348220987" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10370919399225026523"><br/><b>
  <i>Tiffany Reisz is a Goddess with a pen! <br/>5+ Brilliant Stars!</i>
</b><br/><br/>The Original Sinners series by Tiffany Reisz has completely consumed me. This is hands down one of the best series I have had the pleasure of reading. Reisz is brilliant in her writing and capturing the distinct personalities of each of her characters. She writes characters that are multi-layered, that will find their way into your heart and mind. They are dark, funny, witty, charming, promiscuous, damaged, sexy, shy, and just an abso</span>
  <span id="freeText10370919399225026523" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>Tiffany Reisz is a Goddess with a pen! <br>5+ Brilliant Stars!</i>
</b><br><br>The Original Sinners series by Tiffany Reisz has completely consumed me. This is hands down one of the best series I have had the pleasure of reading. Reisz is brilliant in her writing and capturing the distinct personalities of each of her characters. She writes characters that are multi-layered, that will find their way into your heart and mind. They are dark, funny, witty, charming, promiscuous, damaged, sexy, shy, and just an absolutely delicious cast to read. It seems Reisz has come up with her own formula and is very clever in her execution.<br><br>For those that are new to this series, and haven’t read the first book ,The Siren, you must start there, this book is not stand alone. Also, take everything you believe about sex, love, promiscuity, religion and BDSM, particularly S&amp;M, and put it away. If you are not willing to open your mind to a darker story and withhold judgment then this series isn’t for you.<br><br> This story begins a little over a year after The Siren, and life is good for Nora and Soren that is until trouble shows up at Sacred Heart in the form of reporter named Suzanne. Soren is being considered for a promotion to bishop, and Suzanne has received an anonymous fax suggesting a conflict of interest involving the good priest. Of course her first thoughts are that Soren is a pedophile. Soren decides to send Nora and 17 year old Michael to Upstate New York to stay with her friend Griffin until things cool down with the nosey reporter. Soren suggests that Nora take this time to train young Michael as a submissive. This sets in motion a crazy fun ride with Griffin and Nora at the helm. Griffin is the carefree, fun loving, playboy , and was such a fun character to get to know, I just adored him. Nora is magnificent as usual, funny, charming, insightful, and very sweet with those she cares for. Soren, I have a love/hate relationship with, I hate I love him! Then there’s Michael, he’s so sweet, and has such battered self-esteem and self worth.<br><br>Nora hasn’t spent any time away from Soren since she went back to him a little over a year ago. Now in Upstate New York with her friends, her thoughts start to stray back to a young man that she has loved , and has been her best friend. A young man she pushed away so she wouldn’t keep hurting him. I loved this part of the story, there was a moment my heart was just soaring!<br><br>A lot of information from Soren and Nora’s past come out in this book, matter of fact, there’s something revealed about everyone in this story, some of it is dark, and there are some surprises as well. One thing I have noticed in this series, is that characters all come from a damaged past, but that is not why they like the kink they do, they do because it’s just part of their make up, who they are. They would be kinky even without the scars from their past.<br><br> I loved the first book so much and loved this one just as much. The Siren was a bit darker, but The Angel still has the dark element, but is also more flirty and humorous.<br>I actually laughed a lot with this book, and enjoyed every page. This series has landed on my very favorites shelf, and one I could read over and over. The Original Sinners and Tiffany Reisz go beyond stars for me. I give my 5 stars, but it was so much more. Fans of the series will not be disappointed!<br><br>Many Thanks to Harlequin and Netgalley for the advance copy.<br> <br><b>Our interview with Tiffany Reisz</b><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/2012/08/welcome-tiffany-reisz-interview-and.html">http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/20...</a><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704485.The_Prince__The_Original_Sinners___3_" title="The Prince (The Original Sinners, #3) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1344776840s/15704485.jpg" alt="The Prince (The Original Sinners, #3) by Tiffany Reisz" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>Book 3, Expected publication November 2012</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10370919399225026523" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_671823689" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/671823689" />
    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/671823689?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer671823689" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8856012883863436893"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429781i/861209._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Fetishes… they’re the pet you feed or the beast that eats you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429781i/861210._SY540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>How to even find the words to do this series justice?</i><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429781ra/861211.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Raw, dark and <b>real</b>, <i>The Original Sinners</i> is a must read for everyone. Tiffany Reisz draws you in with her captivating story, complex characters and out-of-the-blue turns. <br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “My confession begins,” Father S said, “as the confessions of many men begin– with three words.”<br/>“Father, forgive me?” Michael hazarded a guess.<br/>“I met Eleanor.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><i>The Angel</i> picks up about a </span>
  <span id="freeText8856012883863436893" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429781i/861209._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Fetishes… they’re the pet you feed or the beast that eats you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429781i/861210._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>How to even find the words to do this series justice?</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429781ra/861211.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Raw, dark and <b>real</b>, <i>The Original Sinners</i> is a must read for everyone. Tiffany Reisz draws you in with her captivating story, complex characters and out-of-the-blue turns. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “My confession begins,” Father S said, “as the confessions of many men begin– with three words.”<br>“Father, forgive me?” Michael hazarded a guess.<br>“I met Eleanor.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><i>The Angel</i> picks up about a year after Nora makes the decision to go back to Søren. It’s been a blissful year for her, but with Søren being made one of the contenders to become bishop, she must go away and keep a low profile. However, she won’t be alone. Michael “The Angel” will be joining her and staying at Griffin’s mansion.<br>Once Suzanne Kanter gets an anonymous tip to look into a priest, old memories come to haunt her and she knows she’ll do everything she can to crucify Father Stearns (no pun intended). And she’ll be damned if anything like what happened to her brother happens again. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429781i/861212._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I’m always afraid to start these books. I <i>know</i> that I’m going to be put through the emotional shredder and have one hell of a book hangover. But what I love about this series is that it puts you through hell <b>and makes you enjoy every second of it.</b> It’s rough and raw but there’s always a certain lightheartedness to the story. <br>There are books that you <b>love</b> and you rave about, but after a while you forget certain details or all the feelings you felt while you were reading it begin to dull. This is <b>not</b> the case with <i>The Original Sinners</i>. I can still feel all the love, surprise, heartache… everything. And I know I always will. <br><br>The characters are so complex that you can’t help wanting to know more and getting emotionally invested. Just when you think you’ve solved the mystery that is Nora or Søren, you get slammed in the face with something new. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Why did you leave him?”<br>“Winter,” she finally said, “can be so beautiful and so cruel. Cruel and cold. And if you live in the presence of winter you never have summer.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br>Nora is as wonderful as ever. It’s truly a joy reading about her. She has so much pain but still manages to keep me smiling. <br>Michael and Griffin were great additions to the book. They had a beautiful relationship and you can’t help but me moved by it. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “I want to own you" Griffin whispered into Michael's ear. Michael smiled and for the first time in his life knew exactly what to say and how to say it. "You already do.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Søren is as much as an enigma as ever. I don’t think I’ll ever solve the puzzle that is Søren, and with some of the secrets that came out in <i>The Angel</i> I’m not sure I want to. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429781ra/861213.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> Scar tissue, she’d once read, was the strongest of all tissue. Maybe Søren’s heart was so strong because it was so scarred. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>But I still love him. Forget Wesley, Søren is <b>mine.</b><br>Mwahahahahahahahahahaha nobody else can have him. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/446305.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Except, maybe, Nora… maybe. <br> <br>I didn’t really like Suzanne but I’m biased. As Nora said, why couldn’t she have been ugly? I’m just hoping she doesn’t make a reappearance. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> Father Stearns and Nora Sutherlin had something, a connection, an intimacy… something deep and unexplainable, something untouchable, unreachable. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429781ra/861214.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>In short, if you haven’t read this yet then get started! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “You still love him, don’t you?”<br>“Many waters…”<br>“I never saw you cry over him, that year you were here. Not one tear.”<br>“Some hurts are too deep for tears.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><b>Michael "The Angel"</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429781i/861215._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Søren</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426748i/852943._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Nora</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426748i/852940._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Griffin</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429781i/861216._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>___________________________________________<br> <br><b>My Original Sinners Reviews:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/650795807" rel="nofollow noopener">The Siren (The Original Sinners, #1)</a><br>_______________________________________</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8856012883863436893" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
