<div id="review_3037059162" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3037059162" />
    <a title="Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus"><img alt="Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1456615487p2/52957386.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3037059162?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~" href="/user/show/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus">Melanie A. ~mostly on hiatus~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=library">library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=smutastic">smutastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=unequal-power-dynamic">unequal-power-dynamic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52957386-melanie-a-mostly-on-hiatus?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3037059162" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14267298223369903013">First read: February 2015 - 5 STARS!<br/><b>Re-read: November 2019 - 4 STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>There was something to be said for fighting for the one you loved.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>This installment of <i>The Original Sinners</i> is a pretty good example of why I try to avoid re-reads. But don't worry, I didn't hate it by any means. Reisz's brilliance got the opportunity to shine on multiple occassions . . . <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Fetishes . . . they're the pet you feed or the beast that eats you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>. . . and I ate it up!<br/><br/>Griffin and Michael were b</span>
  <span id="freeText14267298223369903013" style="display:none">First read: February 2015 - 5 STARS!<br /><b>Re-read: November 2019 - 4 STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>There was something to be said for fighting for the one you loved.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>This installment of <i>The Original Sinners</i> is a pretty good example of why I try to avoid re-reads. But don't worry, I didn't hate it by any means. Reisz's brilliance got the opportunity to shine on multiple occassions . . . <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Fetishes . . . they're the pet you feed or the beast that eats you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>. . . and I ate it up!<br /><br />Griffin and Michael were by far my favorite part of the re-read because they provided the only romance; their wonderful chemistry and connection bled from the pages. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Love is the wound that you hope never heals."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> Nora was still Nora. 😍 And the reader is given a few bread crumbs of insight into her relationship with Søren. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Winter," she finally said, "can be so beautiful and so cruel. Cruel and cold. And if you live in the presence of winter you never have summer."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> Also, I liked that Søren got more page time in this book and that another layer was added to his character in the form of a sarcastic streak. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Priests are required to be chaste. Not blind."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> I think the reason I had to lower my rating came down to this: shocking revelations are never as good the second time around. And without the shock factor, I have to admit I found the revelations to be very OTT and bordering on sensationalist.<br /><br />But hey, if literary kink is your thing, this series is not to be missed!<br /><br />This was a 5-way buddy read with the fabulous <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/40572117" rel="nofollow noopener">MONIQUE</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58429822" rel="nofollow noopener">URSY</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14379473" rel="nofollow noopener">LEILA</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/66575688" rel="nofollow noopener">WHITNEY.</a> Thank you so much ladies!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14267298223369903013" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_718103013" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/718103013" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/718103013?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=hot">hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=my-top-reads">my-top-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718103013" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5881377209994248068"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436428i/882078.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><i>The Angel</i> takes place a year after the end of The Siren......<br/><br/>Nora enjoys sex and enjoys it with different people.. this isn't your usual romance story but it's her story... her desires<br/><br/>Once again we get a story full of delicious erotically charged situations, shown to us in such beautiful detail... and a story that explores the unusual in human desires...... again I will not spoil the story with my review, I just have a few thoughts.... okay..... scratch that... a lot of thoughts.... I have a lot</span>
  <span id="freeText5881377209994248068" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436428i/882078.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>The Angel</i> takes place a year after the end of The Siren......<br><br>Nora enjoys sex and enjoys it with different people.. this isn't your usual romance story but it's her story... her desires<br><br>Once again we get a story full of delicious erotically charged situations, shown to us in such beautiful detail... and a story that explores the unusual in human desires...... again I will not spoil the story with my review, I just have a few thoughts.... okay..... scratch that... a lot of thoughts.... I have a lot to say!!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436428i/882079.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series, for me, raises questions about morality, about love.... What do I think is acceptable and right between two people...??? What would I be comfortable with??? It also, undoubtedly, raises questions about the Catholic Faith….. <br><br><b>
  <i>"You have a distinctly Catholic look in your eyes......Guilt."</i>
</b> If you're a Catholic you'll totally get this.... it made me laugh with mirth, it's so true... I will leave Catholicism here…..<br><br><br><i>What would happen if their affair was revealed??? <br>***There would be far reaching consequences in many areas....</i><br><br><b>
  <i>Soren</i>
</b> has the opportunity of a new job; a promotion that would change everything and put life as they know it, at risk... <br><br><b>
  <i>Suzanne</i>
</b>.... our antagonist.... is a reporter sent to uncover Soren??? But what is she meant to discover??? And who tipped her off??? She's incredibly attracted to Soren... he's blond, tall, striking....and staggeringly charismatic..... Who wouldn't be attracted??? <br><br><b>
  <i>"Extremely intelligent and<br> ridiculously handsome."</i>
</b><br><br> Suzanne has been <b>
  <i>Soren-ed.</i>
</b><br><br> <br><b>
  <i>"Soren is a sadist and a dominant."</i>
</b> <br><br>Soren never seems to get and angry, he's very calm and has a <b>
  <i> "...peace and certainty," </i>
</b> aura about him, he's the master of control. And he's so wise and all knowing, like he's of some higher power... in some ways it's quite spooky.....<br><br><b>
  <i>"In their huge underground kinky community, no one commanded more respect or fear than Soren."</i>
</b><br><br>We learn a lot more about his family life, how he came into the world, details about his sister....his mother.... his father... the things he's sacrificed.... when Soren tells his story it gave me goosebumps..... Is this why he is who he is??? Or would he have had certain desires and proclivities anyway???<br><br>Do I feel sympathy for his choices, his sacrifice...??? Has he really sacrificed anything??? <br><br><b>
  <i>"For Soren, S &amp; M was like air or water-he needed it to function."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"Her body came alive with pain, pain that turned to pleasure as he continued his assault on her."</i>
</b><br><br>This has to be one of my favorite quotes from Nora, it made me laugh...... To a member of the church congregation she says, <i>
  <b>"If it's an abomination, it's because your doing it wrong. Bear down hard, then relax. It'll fit better." </b>
</i> <br><br>As well as having a great sense of humor, Nora is caring and fiercely loyal and has an immense capacity to love..... my question is, and I still don't know the answer my heart wants, who exactly should she love????? Should she love and be with Soren???? What about Wesley???<br><br>I feel like she doesn't think she deserves anything more than she has... I get that from the character... I think.... and not my pre-conceived ideals<b>
  <i> "...wanted him....not for the sex. For something else so much deeper and scarier...."</i>
</b> Surely she could have it all with Wes to some degree????<br><br>Wesley is there in the background of this book, not a main feature but a definite presence. We find out a little more about him also...<br><br><i>But... Soren??? Soren?? Soren??? I'm so bloody confused????</i> <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436428i/882082.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The one thing I find really hard to get my head around is....<br><br><b>
  <i>"Since he owned her, he could lend her out and she'd still be his."</i>
</b><br><br><i>What????? </i><br><br><b>
  <i>"...as long as no one hurt her-that was his job alone." </i>
</b><br>It's almost like the pain is the highest level of intimacy???<br><br><i>Sharing</i>..... such intimate moments shared with more people than I, or society, would consider normal yet there was something so tender about it in one particular place...???? I don't understand.... but....???<br><br>Is it the constraints society puts on us that makes us think their sharing lifestyle is wrong....? Is it so wrong if that's what they both want?? They are open and honest, there's no sneaking around... it's not for me personally, but maybe it's perfect for some? Maybe it could be liberating for some?<br><br>I don't understand their relationship but it seems to work for, Nora and Soren and other characters is this book... sharing, sexual infidelity, extreme BDSM.... <br><br>The most shocking act <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ blood play  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was so raw and intimate... Nora and Soren have a closeness and an awareness of each other that is untouchable...it's deep.... and if I'm honest it touched my heart at times. Whilst Soren is not for me, I'm completely invested in them as a couple and at certain points I felt like my heart was routing for them to be together in the strange world they seem to thrive in. They're not <b>harming</b> anyone and only <b>hurting</b> themselves.<br><br>♥<br><br><b>
  <i>Griffin Fiske</i>
</b> is laird of the manor. Tattooed, playboy millionaire and one time druggie... boy did he shine in this book. He shone so bright, I was completely enamored with him and his story. <br><br><b>
  <i>Michael</i>
</b>.....Your heart breaks for Michael and with that heart break comes a want..... to understand him and his S &amp; M lifestyle choice... <br><br><b>
  <i>"Michael is absolutely, completely, ridiculously beautiful." </i>
</b>and for me that's both inside and out...... He's so young but his story of self discovery about who he is and who he needs to be was touchingly beautiful. To see it unfold, the realization for him….. the belief in himself....just stunning.... <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436428i/882083.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"Love was fcuking terrifying." ~ Michael</i>
</b><br><br><br>One of the most memorable things for me was the emergence of the most amazing relationship between <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Michael &amp; Griffin  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> All of their scenes left me wanting more of them and more for them... their love to me was stunning and powerful.... I had feelings of sadness and disbelief towards the dad and to people who cannot accept <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ same sex  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> relationships.... love is love..... this led me to think, well.... what is wrong with the lifestyle Soren and Nora choose.... I don't understand the sharing and the extreme pain and other activities ....why would they want that??? But shouldn't we just accept that it is there way.... love is love..... just a thought... <br><br>The author shows us through the eyes of all the characters. She gives us a pick n mix.... who's <i>the</i> one???<br> <br><b>
  <i>"She seemed to be something of a man-collector."</i>
</b><br><br>I love and adore the way Nora's mind wonders off into the past to give us glimpses and insight into all the major characters. It fleshes out the story creates ambiance... lets us understand why... provides years of information in a show and not tell kind of way. Nora pulls us in and out of her past effortlessly. <br><br>Tiffany Reisz shows, shows and then shows some more, she gives us amazing descriptions so we see them but as well as seeing them we feel them. I started to feel Soren... feel things about him I maybe shouldn't... I'm still not completely his but...???<br><br><b>This author is taking me on some kind of amazing man character journey, destination unknown......and I'm loving every single kinky minute ♥I'm fighting against being <i>Soren-ed</i> but I can feel it coming....</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436428i/882084._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_3152297005" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3152297005" />
    <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers"><img alt="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581473939p2/74622641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3152297005?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers">Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=contem-new-adult-romance">contem-new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=h-s-that-cheated-or-cheats">h-s-that-cheated-or-cheats</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=dom-sub">dom-sub</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3152297005" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16113264754836987047">Well, another book that is only 3 stars that I paid $6.99+tax on. Which I am not thrilled about.<br/><br/>But the strangest thing is that I MAY DO IT AGAIN!!<br/><br/>So... now that I've adjusted my expectations and realized that this series is NOT about romance and TRUE LOVE and all that wonderful warm fuzzies I like to escape to in my reading, I'm less critical about the <b>*everyone sleeps with everyone else*</b> bit.<br/><br/>Why 3 stars then?<br/><br/>BECAUSE:<br/><br/><b>1) I dislike Nora. </b><br/><br/>When a reader dislikes the MC the series is based off of TH</span>
  <span id="freeText16113264754836987047" style="display:none">Well, another book that is only 3 stars that I paid $6.99+tax on. Which I am not thrilled about.<br /><br />But the strangest thing is that I MAY DO IT AGAIN!!<br /><br />So... now that I've adjusted my expectations and realized that this series is NOT about romance and TRUE LOVE and all that wonderful warm fuzzies I like to escape to in my reading, I'm less critical about the <b>*everyone sleeps with everyone else*</b> bit.<br /><br />Why 3 stars then?<br /><br />BECAUSE:<br /><br /><b>1) I dislike Nora. </b><br /><br />When a reader dislikes the MC the series is based off of THE MC, it's hard to give any book in the series anything more than 3 stars. Why do I dislike her? <b>She's a DISLOYAL IMMATURE SEDUCER and MANIPULATOR</b>. <br /><br />Doesn't mean she's a bad person. She's a perfectly fine person who gives her money to good causes, cares about all the men and women she f*cks. All that good stuff. In fact, she reminds me of a friend of mine who's probably slept with 100+ men, don't recall 90% of their names, "loves" maybe 3-4 of them, and she's a good friend, caring person, wonderful all round. <br /><br />BUT. She's not HURTING anyone. <br /><br />Nora DOES hurt people. She hurts Soren and she hurts Wesley and she hurts Kingsley by extension bc of her hold over Soren. I really hate that about her!<br /><br /><b>2)...well, actually Nora is enough to account for the 2 star drop. Everything else is related to her actions that I dislike. </b><br /><br />Soren is devoted enough to her to resist temptation and set her free when he realizes that she loves Wesley. Nora doesn't love either S or W enough to choose and STICK WITH HER CHOICE!! <b>I absolutely abhor triangles. I HATE THEM. They are the anti-love story for me. </b>Anything related to a woman stuck between 2 men or a man stuck between 2 women or a man stuck between 2 men, etc. I can't stand them! It's not true love to me when there's uncertainty and lack of conviction. And I absolutely hate that about Nora.<br /><br />What I liked was the love story between Michael and Griffin. I also liked getting to know Soren: a sadist who is a good man, a great priest, a devoted lover. I want to know more about Kingsley. I may fork over another load of cash to read a book if it's JUST about Kingsley and Soren. I want them to get together and kick Nora to the curb! <br /><br />I don't ever want to read about her again!!<br /><br />(but that's not realistic in this series, so I will have to weigh my next book, if I read any more of this, carefully)</span>
  <a data-text-id="16113264754836987047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('o+hAFnodIx5w09S90l1kPEMFDBMeMg60/u4pAjQguEVsFnfrhliaLXr7lcmiNC57fc+rX1kbYJiJAr5oITIQdQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+kDbBSzAc7dFGSdMoXDCtNqiwkskeeOMCgYVzrHTi4A1vuz40IXKhE8xZjjRGYjz5GhlB2NQjaB96oKkpMEjsA==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15452661011773017225">Tiffany Reisz is the <i>USA Today</i>-bestselling author of the Romance Writers of America RITA®-winning Original Sinners series from Harlequin's Mira Books.<br/><br/>Born in Owensboro, Kentucky, Tiffany graduated from Centre College with a B.A. in English. She began her writing career while a student at Wilmore, Kentucky's Asbury Theological Seminary. After leaving seminary to focus on her fiction, she wrote <i>The </i></span>
  <span id="freeText15452661011773017225" style="display:none">Tiffany Reisz is the <i>USA Today</i>-bestselling author of the Romance Writers of America RITA®-winning Original Sinners series from Harlequin's Mira Books.<br /><br />Born in Owensboro, Kentucky, Tiffany graduated from Centre College with a B.A. in English. She began her writing career while a student at Wilmore, Kentucky's Asbury Theological Seminary. After leaving seminary to focus on her fiction, she wrote <i>The Siren</i>, which has sold more than half a million copies worldwide. <br /><br />Tiffany also writes mainstream women's suspense fiction, including <i>The Bourbon Thief</i> (winner of the <i>RT Book Reviews</i> Seal of Excellence Award) and the RITA®-nominated <i>The Night Mark</i>.<br /><br />Her erotic fantasy <i>The Red</i>—self-published under the banner 8th Circle Press—was named an <i>NPR</i> Best Book of the Year and a Goodreads Best Romance of the Month. It also received a coveted starred review from <i>Library Journal</i>. <br /><br />Tiffany lives in Louisville, Kentucky with her husband, author Andrew Shaffer, and two cats. The cats are not writers. </span>
